Brhadaranyaka-Upanisad (Brhadaranyakopanisad), Kanva recension
with the commentary ascribed to Samkara

ADHYAYA 1


Input by members of the Sansknet project
(formerly: www.sansknet.org)


This GRETIL version has been converted from a custom Devanagari encoding.
Therefore, word boundaries are usually not marked by blanks.
These and other irregularities cannot be standardized at present.

The mula text has been checked against the ed. by V.P. Limaye and R.D. Vadekar
(Eighteen Principal Upanisads, vol. 1, Poona 1958), and the electronic version
available on TITUS. In cases of divergence, preference has usually been given
to the printed edition.

The text of the commentary is not proofread!


REFERENCE SYSTEM:
BrhUp_n,n.n = mula text
BrhUPBh_n,n.n = Samkara's Bhasya

oM
bR^ihadAraNyakopaniShad
oM pUrNamadaH pUrNamidaM pUrNAtpUrNamadacyate /
pUrNasya  pUrNamAdAya  pUrNamevAvashiShyate //
oM shAntiH ! shAntiH !! shAntiH !!!

oM namo brahmAdibhyo brahmavidyAsampradAyakartR^ibhyo vaMshaR^iShibhyo namo gurubhyaH /
'uShA vA ashvasya'ityevamAdyA vAjasaneyibrAhmaNopaniShat /
tasyA iyamalpagranthA vR^ittirArabhyate saMsAravyAvivR^itsubhyaH saMsArahetunivR^ittisAdhanabrahmAtmaikatvavidyApratipattaye /
seyaM brahmavidyA upaniShacchabdhavAcyAtatparANAM sahetoH saMsArasyAtyantAvasAdanAt /
upaniShUvasyasadestadarthatvAt /
tAdarthyAd grantho 'pyupaniShad ucyate /
seyaM  ShaDadhyAyI araNye 'nUcyamAnatvAdAraNyakam,bR^ihattvAtparimANato bR^ihadAraNyakam /
tasyAsya karmakANDena sambandho 'bhidhIyate /
sarvo 'pyayaM vedaH pratyakShAnumAnAbhyAmanavagateShTAniShTaprAptiparihAropAya- prakAshanaparaH sarvapuruShAM nisargata eva tatprAptiparihArayoriShTatvAt /
dR^iShTaviShaye ceShTAniShTaShTaprAptiparihAropAya- j~nAnasya pratyakShAnumAnAbhyAmeva siddatvAnnAgamAnveShaNA /
na cAsati janmAntarasambandhyAtmAstitvavij~nAne janmAntarasambandhyAtmAstitvavij~nAne janmAntareShTAniShTaShTaprAptiparihArecchA syAt svabhAvavAdidarshanAt /
tasmAjjanmAntarasambandhyAtmAstitve janmAntareShTAniShTaShTaprAptiparihAropAyavisheShe ca shAstraM pravartate /
"yeyaM prete vicikitsA mAnuShye 'stItyeke nAyamastIti caike" (ka.u. 1 / 1 / 20) ityupakramya"astItyevopalabdhavyaH"  (ka.u. 2 / 3 / 13) ityevamAdinirNayadarshanAt /
"yathA ca maraNaM prApya" (ka.u.2 / 2 / 6) ityupakramya"yonimanye prapadyante sharIratvAya dehinaH /
sthANumanye 'nusaMyanti yathAkarma yathAshrutam"(ka.u.2 / 2 / 7) iti ca /
"svayaJNjyotiH" (bR^i.u. 4 / 3 / 9) ityupakramya"taM vidyAkarmaNi samanvAramete"( 4 / 4 / 2 ) "puNyo vai puNena karmaNA bhavati pApaH pApena"( 3 / 2 / 13 ) iti ca /
"j~napayiShyAmi"(bR^i.u.2 / 1 / 15) ityupakramya"vij~nAnamayaH"(2 / 1 / 16) iti ca vyatiriktAtmAstitvam /
tatpratyakShaviShayameveti cenna, vAdivipratipattidarshanAt /
na hi dehAntarasambandhina AtmanaH pratyakSheNAstitvavij~nAne lokAyatikA bauddhAshca naH pratikUlAH syunAstyAtmeti vadantaH /
na hi  ghaTAdau pratyakShaviShaye kashcidvipratipadyate nAsti ghaTa iti /
sthANvAdau puruShAdidarshanAnneti cenna nirUpite sthANvAdau vipratipattirbhavati /
vainAshikAstvahamitipratyaye jAyamAne 'pi dehAntaravyatiriktasya nAstitvameva pratijAnate /
tasmAtpratyakShaviShayavailakShaNyAt pratyakShAnnAtmAstitvasiddhiH /
tathAnumAnAdapi /
shrutyA AtmAstitve liN^gasya darshitvAlliN^gasya ca pratyakShaviShayatvAnneti cenna, janmAntarasambandhasyAgrahaNAt /
Agamena tvAtmAstitve 'vagate vedapradarshitalaukikaliN^gavisheShaishca tadanusAriNo mImAMsakAstArkikAshca ahampratyayaliN^gAni ca vaidikAnyeva svamatiprabhavANIti kalpayanto vadanti pratyakShashcAnumeyashcAtmeti /
sarvathApyastyAtmA dehAntarasambandhItyevaM pratipatturdehAntaragateShTAniShTaprAptiparihAropAyavisheShArthinastadvisheShaj~nApanAya karmakANDamArabdham /
na tvAtmana iShTAniShTaprAptiparihArecchAkAraNamAtmaviShayamaj~nAnaM kartR^ibhoktR^isvarUpAbhimAnalakShaNaM tadviparItabrahmAtmasvarUpavij~nAnenApanItam /
yAvaddhi tannApanIyate tAvadayaM karmaphalarAgadveShAdisvAbhAvikadoShaprayuktaH shAstravihitapratiShiddhAtikrameNApi vartamAno manovAkkAyairdR^iShTAdR^iShTAniShTasAdhanAni adharmasaMj~nakAni karmANyupacinoti bAhulyena, svAbhAvikadoShabalIyastvAt /
tataH sthAvarantAdhogatiH /
kadAcicchAstrakR^itasaMskArabalIyastvam, tato manaAdibhiriShTasAdhanaM bAhulyenopacinoti dharmAkhyam /
tad dvividham-j~nAnapUrvakaM kevalaJNca /
tatra kevalaM pitR^ilokAdiprAptiphalam /
j~nAnapUrvakaM devalokAdibrahmalokAntaprAptiphalam /
tathA ca shAstram-"AtmayAji shreyAndevayAjinaH"(shata.brAhma.) ityAdi /
smR^itishca"dvividham karma vaidikam"(manu.12 / 88) ityAdyA /
sAmye ca dharmAdharmayoH manuShyatvaprAptiH /
evaM brahmAndyA sthAvarAntA svAbhAvikAvidyAdidoShavatI dharmAdharmasAdhanakR^itA saMsAragatirnAmarUpakarmAshrayA /
tadevedaM vyAkR^itaM sAdhyasAdhanarUpaM jagatprAgutpatteravyAkR^itamAsIt /
sa eSha bIjAN^kurAdivadavidyAkR^itaH saMsAra Atmani kriyAkArakaphalAdhyAropalakShaNo 'nAdirananto 'narthaH, ityetasmAdviraktasyAvidyAnivR^ittaye tadviparItabrahmavidyApratipattyarthopaniShadArabhyate /
asya tvashvamedhakarmasambandhino vij~nAnasya prayojanaM yepAmashvamedhe na adhikArasteShAmasmAdeva vij~nAnAt phalaprAptiH /
'vidyayA vA karmaNA vA' "taddhaitallokajideva"(bR^i.u.1 / 3 / 28) ityevamAdishrutibhyaH /
karmaviShayatvameva vij~nAnasyeti cenna,"yo 'shvamedhena yajate ya u cainamevaM veda"iti vikalpashruteH /
vidyAprakaraNe cAmnAnAt karmAntare ca sampAdanadarshanAd vij~nAnAt tatphalaprAptirastItyavagamyate /
sarveShAM ca karmaNAM paraM karmAshvamedhaH samaShTivyaShTiprAptiphalavatvAt tasya ceha brahmavidyAprArambha AmnAnaM sarvakarmaNAM saMsAraviShayatvapradarshanArtham /
tathA ca darshayiShyati phalamashanAyAmR^ityubhAvam /
na nityAnAM saMsAraviShayaphalatvamiti cenna, sarvakarmaphalopasaMhArashruteH /
sarvaM hi patnIsambaddhaM karma /
"jayA me syAt ........etAvAnvai kAmaH"(bR^i.u.1 / 4 / 17) iti nisargata eva sarvakarmaNAM kAmyatvaM darshayitvA, putrakarmAparavidyAnAM ca"manuShyalokaH pitR^iloko devalokaH"(bR^i.u.1 / 5 / 16) iti phalaM darshayitvA, tryannAtmakatAM cAnte upasaMhariShyati"trayaM vA idaM nAma rUpaM karma"(bR^i.u.1 / 6 / 1) iti /
sarvatarmaNAM phalaM vyAkR^itaM saMsAra eveti /
idameva trayaM prAgutpattestarhyavyAkR^itamAsIt /
tadeva punaH sarvaprANikarmavashAdvyAkriyate bIjAdiva vR^ikShaH /
so 'yaM vyAkR^itAvyAkR^itarUpaH saMsAro 'vidyAviShayaH;kriyAkArakaphalAtmakatayA AtmarUpatvenAdhyAropitaH avidyayaiva mUrtAmUrtatadvAsanAtmakaH /
ato vilakShaNo 'nAmarUpakarmAtmako 'dvayo nityashuddhabuddhamuktasvabhAvo 'pi kriyAkArakaphalabhedAdiviparyayeNAvabhAsate /
ato 'smAtkriyAkArakaphalabhedasvarUpAd etAvadidamiti sAdhyasAdhanarUpAdviraktasya kAmAdidoShakarmabIjabhUtAvidyAnivR^ittaye rajjvAmiva sarpavij~nAnApanayAya brahmavidyA Arabhyate /
tatra tAvadashvamedhavij~nAnAya'uShA vA ashvasya'ityAdi /
tatrAshvaviShayameva darshanamucyate prAdhAnyAdashvasya /
prAdhAnyaM ca tannAmAN^kitatvAtkratoH prAjApatyatvAcca /

START BrhUp 1,1.1

#<uShA vA ashvasya medhyasya shiraH |
sUryash cakShur vAtaH prANo vyAttam agnir vaishvAnaraH saMvatsara AtmAshvasya medhyasya |
dyauH pR^iShTham antarikSham udaraM pR^ithivI pAjasyaM dishaH pArshve avAntaradishaH parshava R^itavo 'N^gAni mAsAsh cArdhamAsAsh ca parvANy ahorAtrANi pratiShThA nakShatrANy asthIni nabho mAMsAni |
UvadhyaM sikatAH sindhavo gudA yakR^ic ca klomAnash ca parvatA oShadhayash ca vanaspatayash ca lomAni |
udyan pUrvArdho nimloca¤ jaghanArdhaH |
yad vijR^imbhate tad vidyotate |
yad vidhUnute tat stanayati |
yan mehati tad varShati |
vAg evAsya vAk || BrhUp_1,1.1 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_1,1.1 uShA iti, brAhmo muhUrta uShAH /
vaishabdaH smaraNArthaH prasiddhaM kAlaM smArayati /
shiraH prAdhAnyAt /
shirashca pradhAnaM sharIrAvayavAnAm /
ashvasya medhyasya medhArhasyayaj~niyasyopAH shiraH iti sambandhaH /
karmAN^gasya pashoH saMskartavyatvAt kAlAdidR^iShTayaH shira AdiShu kShipyante /
prAjApatyatvaM ca prajApatidR^iShTyadhyAropaNAt /
kAlalokadevatAtvAdhyAropaNaM ca prajApatitvakaraNaM pashoH /
evaMrUpo hi prajApatiH, viShNatvAdikaraNamiva pratimAdau /
sUryashcakShuH shiraso 'nantaratvAt sUryAdhidaivatatvAcca /
vAtaH prANo vAyusvAbhAvyAt /
vyAttaM vivR^itaM mukhamagnirvaishvAnararH /
vaishvAnara ityagnervisheShaNarm /
vaishvAnaro nAmAgnirvivR^itaM mukhamityartho mukhasyAgnidaivatatvAt /
saMvatsara AtmA, saMvatsaro dvAdashamAsastrayodashamAso vA,AtmAsharIram /
kAlAvayavAnAM ca saMvatsaraH sharIraM cAtmA "madhyaM hyaShAmaN^gAnAmAtmA"iti shruteH /
ashvasya medhyasyeti sarvatrAnupaN^gArthaM punarvacanam /
dyauH pR^iShThamUrdhvatvasAmAnyAt /
antarikShamudaraM suShiratvasAmAnyAt pR^ithivI pAjasyaM pAdasyaM pAjasyamiti varNavyatyayena, pAdAsanasthAnamityarthaH /
dishashcatasro 'pi pArshve pArshvena dishAM sambandhAt /
pArshvayordishAM ca saN^khyAvaiShamyAdayuktamiti cenna, sarvamukhatvopapatterashvasya pArshvAbhyAmeva sarvadishAM sambandhAdadoShaH /
avAntaradisha AgneyyAdyAH parshavaH pArshvAsthIni /
R^itavo 'N^gAni saMvatsarAvayavatvAdaN^gasAdharmyAt /
ahorAtrANi pratiShThAH /
bahuvacanAt prAjApatyadaivapitryamAnuShANi, pratiShThAH pAdAH pratitiShThatyetairiti /
ahorAtrairhi kAlAtmA pratitiShThatyashvasya pAdaiH /
nakShatrANyasthIni shuklatvasAmAnyAt /
nabho nabhaHsthA meghA antarIkShasyodaratvokteH, mAMsAnyudakarudhirasecanasAmAnyAt /
UvadhyaM udarasthamardhajIrNamashanaM sikatA vishliShTAvayavatvasAmAnyAt /
sindhavaH syandanasAmAnyannadyo gudA nADyo bahuvacanAcca /
yakR^iccaklomAnashca hR^idayasyAdhasthAddakShiNottarau mAMsakhaNDau /
klomAna iti nityaM bahuvacanamekasminneva /
parvatAH kAThinyAducchritatvAcca /
oShadhayashca kShudrAH sthAvarA vanaspatayo mahAnto lomAni keshAshca yathAsambhavam /
udyannudgacchanbhavati savitA AmadhyAhnAdashvasya pUrvArdho nAmerUrdhvamityarthaH /
nimlocannastaM yannAmadhyAhnAjjaghanArdho 'parArdhaH pUrvAparatvasAdharmyAt /
yadvijR^imbhate gAtrANi vinAmayati vikShipati tadvidyotate vidyotanaM mukhaghanavidAraNasAmAnyAt /
yadvidhUnute gAtrANi kampayati tatstanayati garjanashabdhasAmAnyAt /
yanmehati mUtraM karotyashvastadvarShati varShaNaM tat secanasAmAnyAt /
vAgeva shabda evAsyAshvasya vAgiti, nAtra kalpanetyarthaH //1//


aharvA iti /
sAvarNarAjatau mahimAkhyau grahAvashvasyAgrataH pR^iShThatashca sthApyete tadviShayamidaM darshanam--

START BrhUp 1,1.2

#<ahar vA ashvaM purastAn mahimAnvajAyata |
tasya pUrve samudre yoniH |
rAtrir enaM pashcAn mahimAnvajAyata |
tasyApare samudre yonir |
etau vA ashvaM mahimAnAv abhitaH sambabhUvatuH |
hayo bhUtvA devAn avahad vAjI gandharvAn arvAsurAn ashvo manuShyAn |
samudra evAsya bandhuH samudro yoniH || BrhUp_1,1.2 ||>#

__________

BrhUpBh_1,1.2 ahaH sauvarNo graho dIptisAmAnyAdvai /
aharashvaM purastAnmahimAnvajAyateti katham? ashvasya prajApatitvAt /
prajApatirhyAdityAdilakShaNo 'hnA lakShyate /
ashvaM lakShayitvAjAyata sauvarNo mahimA graho vR^ikShamanu vidyotate vidyuditi yadvat /
tasya grahasya pUrve pUrvaH samudre samudro yonirvibhaktivyatyayena /
yonirityAsAdanasthAnam /
tathA rAtrI rAjate graho varNasAmAnyAjjaghanyatvasAmAnyAdvA /
enamashvaM pashcAtpR^iShTato mahimAnvajAyata, tasyApare samudre yoniH /
mahimA mahattvAt /
ashvasya hi vibhUtireShA yatsauvarNo rAjatashca grahAvubhayataH sthApyete /
tAvetau vai mahimAnau mahimAkhyau grahAvashvamabhitaH sambabhUvaturuktalakShaNAveva sambhUtau /
itthamasAvashvo mahatvayukta iti punarvacanaM stutyartham /
tathA ca hayo bhUtvetyAdi stutyarthameva /
hayo hinotergatikarmaNo vishiShTagatirityarthaH /
jAtavisheSho vA /
devAnavahad devatvamagamayatprajApatitvAt /
devAnAM vA voDhAbhavat /
natu nindaiva vAhanatvam /
naiSha doShaH, vAhanatvaM svAbhAvikamashvasya /
svAbhAvikatvAducchrAyaprAptirdevAdisambandho 'shvasyeti stutirevaiShA /
tathA vAjyAdayo jAtivisheShAH /
vAjI bhUtvA gandharvAnavahadityanuShaN^gaH /
tathArvA bhUtvAsurAn /
ashvo bhUtvA manuShyAn /
samudra eveti paramAtmA bandhubandhanaM badhyate 'sminniti /
samudro yoniH kAraNamutpattiM prati /
evamasau shuddhayoniH shuddhasthitiriti stUyate /
apsu yonirvA ashvaH iti shruteH prasiddha eva vA samudro yoniH //2//

START BrhUp 1,2.1

#<naiveha kiM canAgra AsIt |
mR^ityunaivedam AvR^itam AsId ashanAyayA |
ashanAyA hi mR^ityuH |
tan mano 'kurutAtmanvI syAm iti |
so 'rcann acarat |
tasyArcata Apo 'jAyanta |
arcate vai me kam abhUd iti |
tad evArkyasyArkatvam |
kaM ha vA asmai bhavati ya evam etad arkyasyArkatvaM veda || BrhUp_1,2.1 ||>#

__________

BrhUpBh_1,2.1 naiveha kiJNcanAgra AsIt /
iha saMsAramaNDale kiJNcana kiJNcidapi nAmarUpapravibhaktavisheShaM naivAsId na babhUva agre prAgutpattermanAdeH /
kiM shUnyameva syAt"naiveha kiJNcana"iti shruteH /
na kAryaM kAraNaM vAsIt /
utpatteshca, utpadyate hi ghaTaH, ataH prAgutpatterghaTasya nAstitvam /
nanu kAraNasya na nAstitvaM mR^itpiNDAdidarshanAt /
yannopalabhyate tasyaiva nAstitA /
astu kAryasya na tu kAraNasya, upalampamAnatvAt /
naH prAgutpatteH sarvAnupalambhAt /
anupalabdhishcedabhAvahetuH sarvasya jagataH prAgutpatterna kAraNaM kAryaM vopalabhyate /
tasmAtsarvasyaivAbhAvo 'stu /
naH"mR^ityunaivedamAvR^itamAsIt"iti shruteH /
yadi hi kiJNcidapi nAsId yenAvriyate yaccAvriyate tadA nAvakShyat'mR^ityunaivedamAvR^itam'iti /
na hi bhavati gaganakusumacchanno vandhyAputra iti /
bravIti ca'mR^ityunaivedamAvR^itamAsIt'iti, tasmAdyenAvR^itaM kAraNena, yaccAvR^itaM kAryaM prAgutpattestadubhayamAsIt, shruteH prAmANyAdanumeyatvAcca /
anumIyate ca prAgutpatteH kAryakAraNayorastitvam;kAryasya hi sato jAyamAnasya kAraNe satyutpattidarshanAt, asati cAdarshanAt /
jagato 'pi prAgutpatteH kAraNAstitvamanumIyate ghaTAdikAraNAstitvavat /
ghaTAdikAraNasyApyasattvameva, anupamR^idya mR^itpiNDAdikaM ghaTAdyanutpatteriti cet? na;mR^idAdeH kAraNatvAt /
mR^itsuvarNAdi hi tatra kAraNaM ghaTarucakAdeH, na piNDAkAravisheShaH, tadabhAve bhAvAt /
asatyapi  piNDAkAravisheShe mR^itsuvarNAdikAraNadravyamAtrAdeva ghaTarucakAdikAryotpattirdR^ishyate /
tasmAnna  piNDAkAravisheShe ghaTarucakAdikAraNam /
asati tu mR^itsuvarNAdidravye ghaTarucakAdirna jAyata iti mR^itsuvarNAdidravyameva kAraNam, na tu piNDAkAravisheShaH /
sarvaM hi kAraNaM kAryamutpAdayatpUrvotpannasyAtmakAryasya tirodhAnaM kurvatkAryAntaramutpAdayati, ekasminkAraNe yugapadanekakAryavirodhAt /
na ca pUrvakAryopamamarde kAraNasya svAtmopamarde bhavati /
tasmAtpiNDAdyupamarde kAryotpattidarshanamahetuH prAgutpatteH kAraNAsattveH /
piNDAdivyatirekeNa mR^idAderasattvAdayuktamiti cet-piNDAdipUrvakAryopamarde mR^idAdikAraNaM nopamR^idyate, ghaTAdikAryAntare 'pyanuvartate ityetadayuktam;piNDaghaTAdivyatirekeNa mR^idAdikAraNasyAnupalambhAditi cet? na, mR^idAdikAraNAnAM ghaTAdyutpattau piNDAdinivR^ittAvanuvR^ittidarshanAt /
sAdR^ishyAdanvayadarshanaM na kAraNAnuvR^itteriti cenna, piNDAdigatAnAM mR^idAdyavayavAnAmeva ghaTAdau pratyakShatve 'numAnAbhAsAtsAdR^ishyAdikalpanAnupapatteH /
na ca pratyakShAnumAnayorviruddhAvyabhicAritA,pratyakShapUrvakatvAdanumAnasya sarvatraivAnAshvAsaprasaN^gAt /
yadi ca kShaNikaM sarvaM tadevedamiti gamyamAnaM tadbuddherapyanyatadbuddhyapekShatve tasyA apyanyatadbuddhyapekShatvamityanavasthAyAM tatsadR^ishamidamityasyA api buddhermR^ipAtvAtsarvatrAnAshvAsataiva /
tadidambuddhyorapi kartrabhAve sambandhAnupapattiH /
sAdR^ishyAttatsambandha iti cenna, tadidambuddhyoritaretaraviShayatvAnupapatteH /
asati cetaretaraviShayatve sAdR^ishyagrahaNAnupapattiH /
asatyeva sAdR^ishye tadbuddhiriti cenna, tadidambuddhyorapi sAdR^ishyabuddhivadasadviShayatvaprasaN^gAt /
asadviShayatvameva sarvabuddhInAmastviti cenna, buddhibuddherapyasadviShayatvaprasaN^gAt /
tadapyastviti cenna, sarvabuddhInAM mR^iShAtve 'satyabuddhyanupapatteH /
tasmAdasadetatsAdR^ishyAttadbuddhiriti /
ataH siddhaH prAkkAryotpatteH kAraNasadbhAvaH /
kAryasya cAbhivyaktiliN^gatvAt /
kAryasya ca sadbhAvaH prAgutpatteH siddhaH /
kathamabhivyaktiliN^gatvAdabhivyaktiliN^gamasyeti /
abhivyaktiH sAkShAdvij~nAnAlambanatvaprAptiH /
yadvi loke prAvR^itaM tama AdinA ghaTAdivastu tadAlokAdinA prAvaraNatiraskAreNa vij~nAnaviShayatvaM prApnuvatprAksadbhAvaM na vyabhicarati /
tathedamapi jagatprAgutpatterityavagacchAmaH /
na hyavidyamAno ghaTa udite 'pyAditye upalabhyate /
na te 'vidyamAnatvAbhAvAdupalabhyetaiveti cet /
na hi tava ghaTAdikAryaM kadAcidapyavidyamAnamityudite Aditye upalabhyetaiva mR^itpiNDe 'sannihite tamAdyAvaraNe cAsati vidyamAnatvAditi cet? na, dvividhatvAdAvaraNasya /
ghaTAdikAryasya dvividhaM hyAvaraNaM mR^idAdAravibhaktasya tamaHkuDyAdi prAÇmR^ido 'bhivyaktermR^idAdyavayavAnAM piNDAdikAryAntararUpeNa saMsthAnam /
tasmAtprAgutpattervidyamAnasyaiva ghaTAdikAryasya AvR^itatvAdanupalabdhiH /
naShTotpannabhAvAbhAvashabdapratyayabhedastu abhivyAktatirobhAvayordvividhatvApekShaH /
piNDakapAlAderAvaraNavailakShaNyAdayuktamiti cet? tamaHkuDyAdi hi ghaTAdyAvaraNaM ghaTAdibhinnadeshaM dR^iShTaM na tathA ghaTAdibhinnadeshe dR^iShTe piNDakapAle /
tasmAt piNDakapAlasaMsthAnayorvidyamAnasyaiva ghaTasyAvR^itatvAd anupalabdhirityayuktam AvaraNadharmavailakShaNyAditi cet? na kShIrodakAdeH kShIrAdyAvaraNenaikadeshatvadarshanAt /
ghaTAdikArye kapAlacUrNAdyavayavAnAmantarbhAvAdanAvaraNatvamiti cenna, vibhaktAnAM kAryAntaratvAdAvaraNatvopapatteH /
AvaraNAbhAva eva yatnaH kartavya iti cet? piNDakapAlAvasthayorvidyamAnameva ghaTAdikAryamAvR^itatvAnnobhalabhyata iti ced ghaTAdikAryArthinA tadAvaraNavinAsha eva yatnaH kartavyo na ghaTAdyutpattau? na caitadasti, tasmAdayuktaM vidyamAnasyaivAvR^itatvAdanupalabdhiriti cet? na aniyamAt /
na hi vinAshamAtraprayatnAdeva ghaTAdyabhivyaktirniyatA /
tamAdyAvR^ite ghaTAdau pradIpAdyutpattau prayatnadarshanAt /
so 'pi tamonAshAyaiveti cet? dIpAdyutpattAvapi yaH prayatnaH so 'pi tamastiraskaraNAya tasminnaShTe ghaTaH svayamevopalabhyate /
na hi kiJNcidAdhIyate iti cet? na, prakAshavato ghaTasyopalabhyamAnatvAt /
yathA prakAshavishiShTo ghaTa upalabhyate  na tathA prAkpradIpakaraNAt /
tasmAnna tamastiraskArAyaiva pradIpakaraNaM kiM tarhi? prakAshavattvaya /
prakAshavattvenaivopalabhyamAnatvAt /
kvacidAvaraNavinAshe 'pi yatnaH syAt, yathA kuDyAdivinAshe /
tasmAnna niyamo 'styabhivyaktarthinAvaraNavinAsha eva yatnaH kArya iti /
niyamAtmarthavattvAcca /
kAraNe vartamAnaM kAryaM kAryAntarANAmAvaraNamityavocAma /
tatra yadi pUrvAbhivyaktasya kAryasyapiNDasyavyavahitasya vA kapAlasya vinAsha eva yatnaH kriyeta, tadA vidalacUrNAdyapi kAryaM jAyeta /
tenApyAvR^ito ghaTo nopalabhyata iti  punaH prayatnAntarapekShaiva /
tasmAd ghaTAdyabhivyaktyarthino niyata eva kArakavyApAror'thavAn /
tasmAtprAgutpatterapi tadeva kAryam /
atitAnAgatapratyayabhedAcca /
atIto ghaTo 'nAgato ghaTa ityetayoshca pratyayorvartamAnaghaTapratyayavanna nirviShayatvaM yuktam;anAgatArthipravR^itteshca /
na hyasatyarthitayA pravR^ittirloke dR^iShTA /
yoginAM cAtItAnAgataj~nAnasya satyatvAt /
asaMshcedbhaviShyadghaTa aishvarambhaviShyadghaTaviShayaM pratyakShaj~nAnaM mithyA syAt na ca pratyakShamupacaryate /
ghaTasadbhAvehyanumAnamavocAma /
vipratiShedhAcca /
yadi ghaTo bhaviShyatIti kulAlAdiShu vyApriyamANeShu ghaTArthaM pramANena nishcitaM yena ca kAlena ghaTasya sambandho bhaviShyatItyucyate, tasminneva kAle ghaTo 'sanniti vipratiShiddhamabhidhIyate /
bhaviShyanaghaTo 'sanniti, na bhaviShyatItyarthaH /
ayaM ghaTo na vartata iti yadvat /
atha prAgutpatterghaTo 'sannityucyeta, ghaTArtha pravR^itteShu kulAlAdiShu tatra yathA vyApArarUpeNa vartamAnAstAvatkulAlAdayaH, tathA ghaTo na vartata ityasacchabdasyArthashcenna virudhyate /
kasmAt? svena hi bhaviShyadrUpeNa ghaTo vartate /
na hi piNDasya vartamAnatA kapAlasya vA ghaTasya bhavati /
na ca tayorbhaviShyattA ghaTasya /
tasmAtkulAlAdivyApAravartamAnatAyAM prAgutpatterghaTo 'sanniti na virudhyate /
yadi ghaTasya yatsvaM bhaviShyattAkAryarUpaM tatpratipidhyeta, tatpratipedhe virodhaH syAt /
na tu tadbhavAnpratiShedhati /
na ca sarveShAM kriyAvatAM kArakANAmekaiva vartamAnatA bhaviShyattvaM vA /
api ca caturvidhAnAmabhAvAnAM ghaTasyetaretarAbhAvo ghaTAdanyo dR^iShTo yathA ghaTAbhAvaH paTAdireva na ghaTasvarUpameva /
na ca ghaTAbhAvaH sanpaTo 'bhAvAtmakaH, kiM tarhi? bhAvarUpa eva /
evaM ghaTasya prAkpradhvaMsAtyantAbhAvanAmapi ghaTAdanyatvaM syAt /
ghaTena vyapadishyamAnatvAd  ghaTasyetaretarAbhAvavat /
tathaiva bhAvAtmakatAbhAvAnAm /
evaM ca sati ghaTasya prAgabhAva iti na ghaTasvarUpameva prAgutpatternAsti /
atha ghaTasya prAgabhAva iti ghaTasya yatsvarUpaM tadevocyeta ghaTasyetivyapadeshAnupapattiH /
atha kalpayitvA vyapadishyeta shilAputrakasya sharIramiti yadvat, tathApi ghaTasya prAgabhAva iti kalpitasyaivAbhAvasya ghaTena vyapadesho na ghaTasvarUpasyaiva /
athArthAntaraM ghaTAd ghaTasyAbhAva iti, uktottarametat /
kiJNcAnyatprAgutpatteH shashaviShANavadabhAvabhUtasya ghaTasya svakAraNasattAsambandhAnupapattiH, dviniShThatvAtsambandhasya ayutasiddhAnAmadoSha iti cenna, bhAvAbhAvayorayutasiddhatvAnupapatteH /
bhAvAbhUtayorhi yutasiddhatAyutasiddhatA vA syAnna tu bhAvAbhAvayorabhAvayorvA /
tasmAtsadeva kAryaM prAgutpatteriti siddham /
kiMllakShaNena mR^ityunAvR^itamityata Aha-ashanAyayA ashitumicchA ashanAyA saiva? mR^ityorlakShaNaM tayA lakShitena mR^ityunAshanAyayA /
kathamashanAyA mR^ityuH? ityucyate-- ashanAyA hi mR^ityuH /
hishabdena prasiddhaM hetumavadyotayati /
yo hyashitumicchati so 'shanAyAnantarameva hanti jantUn, tenAsAvashanAyayA lakShyate mR^ityurityashanAyA hItyAha /
buddhyAtmano 'shanAyA dharma iti sa eSha buddhyavastho hiraNyagarbho mR^ityurityucyate /
tena mR^ityunedaM kAryamAvR^itamAsIt /
yathA piNDAvasthayA mR^idA ghaNTAdaya AvR^itAH syuriti tadvat /
tanmano 'kuruta /
taditi manaso nirdeshaH /
sa prakR^ito mR^ityurvakShyamANakAryasisR^ikShayA tatkAryAlocanakShamaM manaHshabdavAcyaM saMkalpAdilakShaNamantaHkaraNamakuruta kR^itavAn /
kenAbhiprAyeNa mano 'karot? ityucyate-AtmanvI AtmavAn syAM bhaveyam /
ahamanenAtmanA manasA manasvI syAmityabhiprAyaH /
sa prajApatirabhivyaktena manasA samanaskaH sannarcannarcayanpUjayan AtmAnameva kR^itArtho 'smItyacaraccaraNamakarot /
tasya prajApaterarcataH pUjayata Apo rasAtmikAH pUjAN^gabhUtA ajAyantotpannAH /
atrAkAshaprabhR^itInAM trayANAmutpattyanantaramiti vaktavyam, shrutyantarasAmarthyAdvikalpAsambhavAcca sR^iShTikramasya /
arcate pUjAM kurvate vai me mahyaM kamudakamabhUdityevamamanyata yasmAnmR^ityuH, tadeva tasmAdeva hetorarkasya agnerashvamedhakratvaupayogikasyArkatvam arkatve heturityarthaH /
agnerarkanAmanirvacanametet /
arcanAtsukhahetupUjAkaraNAd apsambandhAcca agneretadgauNaM nAmArka iti /
ya evaM yathoktamarkasyArkatvaM veda jAnAti kamudakaM sukhaM vA nAmasAmAnyAt /
ha vA ityavatAraNArthau /
bhavatyeveti /
asmai evaMvide evaMvidarthaM bhavati //1//

BrhUpBh_1,2.4 sa mR^ityurakAmayata kAmitavAn /

START BrhUp 1,2.7

#<so 'kAmayata -- medhyaM ma idaM syAd Atmanvy anena syAm iti |
tato 'shvaH samabhavat |
yad ashvat tan medhyam abhUd iti tad evAshvamedhasyAshvamedhatvam |

eSha vA ashvamedho ya eSha tapati |
tasya saMvatsara AtmA |
ayam agnir arkaH |
tasyeme lokA AtmAnaH |
tAv etAv arkAshvamedhau |
so punar ekaiva devatA bhavati mR^ityur eva |
apa punarmR^ityuM jayati |
nainaM mR^ityur Apnoti |
mR^ityur asyAtmA bhavati |
sarvam Ayur eti |
etAsAM devatAnAm eko bhavati || BrhUp_1,2.7 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_1,2.7 so 'kAmayata, katham? medhyaM medhArha yaj~niyaM me mamedaM sharIraM syAt /
kiJNca AtmanvyAtmavAMshcAnena sharIreNa sharIravAnsyAmiti prAvivesha /
yasmAttaccharIraM tadviyogAdgatayashorvIryaM sad ashvad ashvayat tatastasmAdashvaH samabhavat /
tato 'shvanAmA prajApatireva sAkShAditi stUyate /
yasmAcca punastatpraveshAdgatayashovIryatvAdamedhyaM sanmedhyamabhUttadeva tasmAdevAshvamedhasyAshvamedhanAmnaH kratorashvamedhatvam ashvamedhanAmalAbhaH /
kriyAkArakaphalAtmako hi kratuH /
sa ca prajApatireveti stUyate /
kratunirvartakasyAshvasya pajApatitvamuktam'uShA vA ashvasya medhasya'ityAdinA /
tasyaivAshvasya medhyasya prajApatisvarUpasyAgneshca yathoktasya kratuphalAtmarUpatayA samasyopAsanaM vidhAtavyamityArabhyate /
pUrvatra kriyApadasyavidhAyakasyAshrutatvAt kriyApadApekShatvAcca prakaraNasya ayamartho 'vagamyate /
eSha ha ashvamedhaM kratuM veda ya enamevaM veda, yaH kashcidenamashvamagnirUpamarkaM ca yathoktamevaM vakShyamANena samAsena padarshyamAnena visheShaNena vishiShTaM veda, sa eSho 'shvamedhaM veda nAnyaH /
tasmAdevaM veditavya ityarthaH /
katham? tatra pashuviShayameva tAvaddarshanamAha /
tatra prajApatirbhUyasA yaj~nena bhUyo yajeyeti kAmayitvA AtmAnameva pashuM medhyaM kalpayitvA taM pashumanavarudhyaivotsR^iShTaM pashumavarodhamakR^ityaiva muktapragrahamamanyatAcintayat /
taM saMvatsarasya pUrNasya parastAdUrdhvamAtmane AtmArthamAlabhata- prajApatidevatAkatvenetyetat- AlabhatAlambhaM kR^itavAn /
pashUnanyAngrAmyAnAraNyAMshca devatAbhyo yathAdaivataM pratyauhatpratigamitavAn /
yasmAccaivaM prajApatiramanyata tasmAdevamanyo 'pyuktena vidhinAtmAnaM pashumashvaM medhyaM kalpayitvA- sarvadevatyo 'haM prokShyamANa AlabhyamAnastvahaM maddevatya eva syAm, anya itare pashavo grAmyAraNyA yathAdaivatamanyAbhyo devatAbhya Alabhyante madavayavabhUtAbhya eva- itividyAt /
ata evedAnIM sarvadevatyaM prokShitaM prAjApatyamAlabhante yAj~nikAH /
'evameva ha vA ashvamedho ya eSha tapati'- yastvevaM pashusAdhanakaH kratuH sa eSha sAkShAtphalabhUto nirdishyata eSha ha vA ashvamedhaH /
ko 'sau? ya eva savitA tapati jagadavabhAsayati tejasA /
tasyAsya kratuphalAtmanaH saMvatsaraH kAlavisheShaH, AtmA sharIraM tannirvartyatvAtsaMvatsarasya /
tasyaiva kratvAtmanaH, agnisAdhyatvAcca phalasya kratutvarUpeNaiva nirdeshaH, ayaM pArthivo 'gnirarkaH sAdhanabhUtaH /
tasya cArkasya kratau cityasyeme lokAstrayo 'yopyAtmAnaH sharIrAvayavAH /
tathA ca vyAkhyAtaM'tasya prAcI dik'ityAdinA /
tAvagnyAdityAvetau yathAvisheShitAvarkAshvamedhau kratuphale /
arko yaH pArthivo 'gniH sa sAkShAtkraturUpaH kriyAtmakaH /
kratoragnisAdhyatvAttadrUpeNaiva nirdeshaH /
kratusAdhyatvAcca phalasya kraturUpeNaiva nirdesha Adityo 'shvamedha iti /
tau sAdhyaisAdhanau kratuphalabhUtAvagnyAdityau, sA u punarbhUya ekaiva devatA bhavati /
kA sA? mR^ityureva /
pUrvamapyekaivAsItkriyAsAdhanaphalabhedAya vibhaktA /
tathA coktam"sa tredhAtmAnaM vyakuruta" (bR^i.u.1 / 2 / 3) iti /
sA punarapi kriyAnirvR^ittyuttarakAlamekaiva devatA bhavati mR^ityureva phalarUpa /
yaH punarevamenamashvamedhaM mR^ityumekAM devatAM veda /
ahameva mR^ityurasmyashvamedha ekA devatA madrUpA ashvAgnisAdhanasAdhyeti so 'pajayati punarmR^ityuM punarmaraNaM sakR^inmR^itvA punarmaraNAya na jAyata ityarthaH /
apajito 'pi mR^ityurenaM punarApnuyAdityAshaN^kyAha- nainaM mR^ityurApnoti /
kasmAt? mR^ityurasya evaMvida AtmA bhavati /
kiJNca mR^ityureva phalarUpaH sanne tAsAM devatAnAmeko bhavati /
tasyaitat phalam //7//

#<iti prathamAdhyAye dvitIyamagnibrAhmaNam //2//>#



dvayA hetyAdyasya kaH sambandhaH? karmaNAM j~nAnasahitAnAM parA gatiruktA mR^ityvAtmabhAvo 'shvamedhagatyuktyA /
athedAnIM mR^ityvAtmabhAvasAdhanabhUtayoH karmaj~nAnayoryata udbhavastatprakAshanArthamudgIthabrAhmaNamArabhyate /
nanu mR^ityvAtmabhAvaH pUrvatra j~nAnakarmaNoH phalamuktam /

nAyaM doShaH;agnyAdityAtmabhAvatvAdudgIthaphalasya /
pUrvatrApyetadeva phalamuktam'etAsAM devatAnAmeko bhavati'iti /

ko 'sau   svAbhAvikaH papmAsaN^go mR^ityuH? kuto vA tasyodbhavaH? kena vA tasyAtikramaNam? kathaM vA? ityetasyArthasya prakAshanAyAkhyAyikArabhate /

#<dvayA ha prAjApatyA devAsh cAsurAsh ca tataH kAnIyasA eva devA jyAyasA asurAH |

te ha devA Ucur hantAsurAn yaj~na udgIthenAtyayAmeti || BrhUp_1,3.1 ||>#

BrhUpBh_1,3.1 dvayA dviprakArAH /
heti pUrvavR^ittAvadyodako nipAtaH /
vartamAna pradApateH pUrvajanmani yad vR^ittaM tadavadyodayati hashabdena /

ke te? devAshcAsurAshca /
tasyaiva prajApateH prANA vAgAdayaH /
kathaM punasteShAM devAsuratvam? ucyate - shAstrajanitaj~nAnakarmabhAvitA dyodanAddevA bhavanti /
ta eva svAbhAvikapratyakShAnumAnajanitadR^iShTaprayojanakarmaj~nAnabhAvitA asurAH /

katham? hantedAnIm asminyaj~ne jyotiShTome, udgIthena udgIthakarmapadArthakartR^isvarUpAshrayaNena AtyayAmAtigacchAmaH /
asurAnabhibhUya svaM devabhAvaM shAstraprakAshitaM pratipatyAmaha ityuktavanto 'nyonyam /
udgIthakarmapadArthakartR^isvarUpAshrayaNaM ca j~nAnakarmabhyAm /
karma vakShyamANaM mantrajapalakShaNaM vidhitsyamAnaM"tadetAni japet"iti /
j~nAnaM tvidameva nirUpyamANam /
nanvidamabhyArohajapavisheShor'thavAdau na j~nAnanirUpaNaparam /
na; 'ya evaM veda'iti vacanAt /
udgIthaprastAve purAkalpashravaNAdudgIthavidhiparamiti cenna, aprakaraNAt /
udgIthasya cAnyatra vihitatvAt /
vidyAprakaratvAccAsya /
abhyArohajapasya cAnityatvAt, evaM viprayojyatvAt;vij~nAnasya ca nityavacchravaNAt /
"taddhaitallokajideva"(bR^i. u.1 / 3 / 28) iti ca shruteH;prANasya vAgAdInAM shuddhyashuddhivacanAt /
na hyanyupAsyate prANasya shuddhivacanaM vAgAdInAM ca sahopAnyastAnAmashuddhivacanam /
vAgAdinindayA mukhyaprANastutishcAbhipretA upapadyate /
'mR^ityumatikrAnto dIpyate'ityAdi phalavacanaM ca /
prANasvarUpApatterhi phalaM tadyadvAgAdyagnyAdibhAvaH /
bhavatu nAma prANasyopAsanam, na tu vishuddhyAdiguNavatteti /
nanu syAcchrutatvAt;na syAt;upAsyatve stutyarthatvopapatteH /
na;aviparItArthapratipatteH shreyaHprAptyupapatterlokavat /
yo hyaviparItamarthaM pratipadyate loke sa iShTaM prApnotyaniShTAdvA nivartate, na viparItArthapratipattyA /
tathehApi shrautashabdajanitArthapratipattau shreyaHprAptirupapannA na viparyaye /

na ca tadvij~nAnasyApavAdaH shrUyate /

yo hi viparyayeNArthaM pratipadyate loke, puruShaM sthANurityamitraM mitramiti vA, so 'narthaM prApnuvandR^ishyate /
AtmeshvaradevatAdInAmapi ayathArthAnAmeva ced grahaNaM shrutitaH, anarthaprAptyarthaM shAstramiti dhruvaM prApnuyAllokavadeva, na caitadiShTam;tasmAdyathAbhUtAneva AtmeshvaradevatAdIn grAhayatyupAsanArthaM shAstram /
nAmAdau brahmadR^iShTidarshanAdayuktamiti cetsphuTaM nAmAderabrahmatvam, tatra brahmadR^iShTiM sthANbAdAviva puruShadR^iShTiM viparItAM grAhayacchAstraM dR^ishyate /
tasmAdyathArthameva shAstrataH pratipatteH shreyaH ityuktamiti cet? na, pratimAvadbhedapratipatteH /
nAmAdavabrahmaNi brahmadR^iShTiM viparItAM grAhayati shAstraM sthANbAdAviva puruShadR^iShTiM, iti naitatsAdhvavocaH /
kasmtAt? bhedena hi brahmaNo nAmAdivastupratipannasya nAmAdau vidhIyate brahmadR^iShTiH pratimAdAviva viShNudR^iShTiH /
Alambanatvena hi nAmAdipratipattiH pratimAdivadeva, na tu nAmAdyeva brahmeti /
yathA sthANAvanirj~nAte na sthANuriti, puruSha evAyamiti pratipadyate viparItam, na tu tathA nAmAdau brahmadR^iShTirviparItA /
brahmadR^iShTireva kevalA nAsti brameti cet /
etena pratimAbrAhmaNAdiShu viShNvAdidevapitrAdidR^iShTInAM tulyatA /
na;R^igAdiShu pR^ithivyAdidR^iShTidarshanAt /
vidyamAnapR^ithivyAdivastudR^iShTInAmeva R^igAdiviShaye kShepadarshanAt /
tasmAttatsAmAnyAnnAmAdiShu brahmAdidR^iShTInAM vidyamAnabrahmAdiviShayatvasiddhiH /
etena pratimAbrAhmaNAdiShu viShNvAdidevapitrAdibuddhInAM ca satyavastuviShayatvasiddhiH /
mukhyApekShatvAcca gauNatvasya /
paJNcAgnyAdiShu cAgnitvAdergauNatvAd mukhyAgnyAdisadbhAvavannAmAdiShu bahmatvasya gauNatvAnmukhyabrahmasadbhAvopapattiH /
kriyArthaishcAvisheShAdvidyArthAnAm yathA ca darshapaurNamAsAdikriyedamphalA vishiShTaitikartavyatAkA evaN^kramaprayuktAN^gA ca ityetadalaukikaM vastu pratyakShAdyaviShayaM tathAbhUtaM ca vedavAkyaireva j~nApyate /
tathA, paramAtmeshvaradevatAdivastu asthUlAdidharmakamashanAyAdyatItaM cetyevamAdivishiShTamiti vedavAkyaireva j~nApyate, ityalaukikatvAttathAbhUtameva bhavitumarhatIti /
na ca kriyArthairvAkyairj~nAnavAkyAnAM buddhyutpAtakatve visheSho 'sti /
na cAnishcitA viparyastA vA paramAtmAdivastuviShayA buddhirutpadyate /
anuShTheyAbhAvAdayuktamiti cet kriyArthairvAkyaistryaMshAbhAvanAnuShTheyA j~nApyate 'laukikyapi /
na tathA paramAtmeshvarAdivij~nAne 'nuShTheyaM kiJNcitasti /
ataH kriyArthaiH sAdharmyamityayuktamiti cet? na, j~nAnasya tathAbhUtArthaviShayatvAt na hyanuShTheyatvAttathAtvam, kiM tarhi? pramANasamadhigatatvAt /
na ca tadviShayAyA buddheranuShTheyaviShayatvAttathArthatvam, kiM tarhi? vedavAkyajanitatvAdeva /
vedavAkyAdhigatasya vastunastathAtve satyanuShTheyatvavishiShThaM cedanutiShThati /
no cedanuShTheyatvavishiShThaM nAnu tiShThati /
ananuShTheyatve vAkyapramANatvAnupapattiriti cet /
na hyanuShTheye 'sati padAnAM sahatirupapadyate /
anuShTheyatve tu sati tAdarthyena padAni saMhanyante /
tatrAnuShTheyaniShThaM vAkyaM pramANaM bhavati idamanenaivaM kartavyamiti /
na tvidamanenaivamityevaM prakArANAM padashatAnAmapi vAkyatvamasti'kuryAtkriyeta kartavyaM bhavetsyAditi paJNcamam'ityevamAdInAmanyatame 'sati /
ataH paramAtmeshvarAdInAmavAkyapramANatvam, padArthatve ca pramANAntaraviShayatvam /
ato 'sadetaditi cet? na,'asti merurvarNacatuShTayopetaH'ityevamAdyananuShTheye 'pi vAkyadarshanAt /

mervAdij~nAnavatparamAtmaj~nAne prayojanAbhAvAdayuktamiti cet? na,"brahmavidApnoti param"(tai.u.2 / 1 / 1) "brahmavidApnoti param bhidyate hR^idayagranthiH"(mu.u.2 / 2 / 8) iti phalashravaNAt, saMsArabIjAvidyAdidoShanivR^ittidarshanAcca /

na cAnuShTheyaH saH /
na ca pratiShiddhaviShaye pravR^ittakriyasya akaraNAdanyadanuShTheyamasti /

kShudhArtasya pratiShedhaj~nAnasaMskR^itasya abhakShye 'bhojye vA pratyupasthite kalajjAbhishastAnnAdau'idaM bhakShyamado bhojyam'iti vA j~nAnamutpannam, tadviShayayA pratiShedhaj~nAnasmR^ityA bAdhyate /
mR^igatR^iShNikAyAmiva peyaj~nAnaM tadviShayayAthAtmyavij~nAnena /

nanu kalaJNjAdibhakShaNAderanarthArthatvavastuyAthAtmyaj~nAnasmR^ityA svAbhAvike tadbhakShyatvAdiviShayaviparItaj~nAne nivartite tadbhakShaNAdyanarthapravR^ittyabhAvavadapratiShedhaviShayatvAcchAstravihitapravR^ittyabhAvo na yukta iti cet /

nanu tatra yuktaH, nityAnAM tu kevalashAstranimittatvAt, anarthArthatvAbhAvaccAbhAvo na yukta iti cet? na avidyArAgadveShAdidoShavato vihitatvAt /
yathA svargakAmAdidoShavato darshapUrNamAsAdIni kAmyAni karmANi vihitAni tathA sarvAnarthabIjAvidyAdidoShavatastajjaniteShTAniShTaprAptiparihArarAgadveShAdidoShavatashca tatpreritAvisheShapravR^itteriShTAniShTaprAptiparihArArthino nityAni karmANi vidhIyante, na kevalaM shAstranimittAnyeva /
na cAgnihotradarshapUrNamAsacAturmAsyapashubandhasomAnAM karmaNAM svataH kAmyanityatvavivekosti /

vishiShTakriyAsAdhanAdij~nAnapUrvakatvAtkriyApravR^itteH /

tasmAt paramAtmAyAthAtmyaj~nAnavidherapi tadviparItasthUladvaitAdij~nAnanivartakatvAt sAmarthyAtsarvakarmapratiShedhavidhyarthatvaM sampadyate;karmapravR^ittyabhAvasya tulyatvAd yathA pratiShedhaviShaye /
tasmAt pratiShedhavidhivacca vastupratipAdanaM tatparatvaM ca siddhaM shAstrasya //1//

#<te ha vAcam Ucus tvaM na udgAyeti |

BrhUpBh_1,3.2 te devA haivaM vinishcitya, vAcaM vAgabhimAninIM devatAmucuruktavantaH /
tvaM no 'smabhyamudgAyaudgAtraM karma kuruShva /
vAgdevatAnirvarttyamaugAtraM kama dR^iShTavantaH, tAmeva ca devatAM japamantrAbhidhAyAm"asato mA sadgamaya"(bR^i.u.1 / 3 / 28) iti /
atra copAsanAyAH karmaNashca kartR^itvena vAgAdaya eva vivakShyante /
kasmAt? yasmAtparamArthatastat kartR^ikastadviShaya eva ca sarvo j~nAnakarmasaMvyavahAraH /
vakShyati hi"dhyAyatIva lelAyatIva"ityAtmakartR^ikatvAbhAvaM vistarataH ShaShTe /
ihApi cAdyAyAnte upasaMhariShyati avyAkR^itAdikriyAkArakaphalajAtam,"trayaM vA idaM nAma rUpaM karma"(1 / 6 / 1) iti avidyAviShayam /
avyAkR^itAttu yatparaM paramAtmAkhyaM vidyAviShayam anAmarUpakarmAtmakam"neti neti"(2 / 3 / 6) iti itarapratyAkhyAnenopasaMhariShyati pR^ithak /
yastu vAgAdisamAhAropAdhiparikalpitaH saMsAryAtmA taM ca vAgAdisamAhArapakShapAtinameva darshayiShyati"etebhyo bhUtebhyaH samutthAya tAnyevAnuvinashyati"(2 / 4 / 12) iti /
tasmAdyuktA vAgAdInAmeva j~nAnakarmakartR^itvaphalaprAptivivakShA /
tatheti tathAstviti devairuktA vAktebhyo 'rthibhyor'thAya udakAyadudgAnaM kR^itavatI /
kaH punarasau devebhyor'thAya udgAnakarmaNA vAcA nirvartitaH kAryavisheShaH? ityucyate- yo vAcI nimittabhUtAyAM vAgAdisamudAyasya ya upakAro niShpadyate vadanAdivyApAreNa, sa eva /
sarveShAM hyasau vAgvadanAbhinirvR^itto bhogaH phalam /
taM bhogaM sA tR^iShu pavamAneShu kR^itvA avashiShTeShu navasu stotreShu vAcanikamArtvijyaM phalaM yatkalyANaM shobhanaM vadati varNAnabhinirvartayati tad Atmane mahyameva /
taddhyasAdhAraNaM vAgdevatAyAH karma yatsamyagvarNAnAmuccAraNam /
atastadeva visheShyate yatkalyANaM vadatIti /
yattu vadanakAryaM sarvasaMghAtopakArAtmakaM tadyAjamAnameva /
tatra kalyANavadanAtmasambandhAsaN^gAvasaraM devatAyA randhraM pratilamya te vidurasurAH, katham? anenodgAtrAno 'smAnsvAbhAvikaM j~nAnaM cAbhibhUyAtItya shAstrajanitakarmaj~nAnarUpeNa jyotiShodgAtrAtmanA atyeShvantyatigamiShyanti /
ityevaM vij~nAya samudgAtAramabhidrutyAbhigamya svena AsaN^galakShaNena pApmanAvidhyaMstADitavantaH saMyojitavanta ityarthaH /
sa yaH sa pApmA prajApateH pUrvajanmAvasthasya vAci kShiptaH sa eSha pratyakShIkriyate /
ko 'sau? yadevamapratirUpamananurUpaM shAstrapratiShiddhaM vadati yena prayukto 'sabhyabIbhatsAnR^itAdyanicchannapi vadati /
anena kAryeNApratirUpavadanena anugamyamAnaH prajApateH kAryabhUtAsu prajAsu vAci vartate /
sa evApratirUpavadanenAnumitaH sa prajApatervAci gataH pApmA, kAraNAnuvidhAyi hi kAryamiti //2//

START BrhUp 1,3.3-6

#<atha ha prANam Ucus tvaM na udgAyeti |
tatheti tebhyaH prANa udagAyat |
yaH prANe bhogas taM devebhya AgAyat |
yat kalyANaM jighrati tad Atmane |
te 'vidur anena vai na udgAtrAtyeShyantIti |
tam abhidrutya pApmanAvidhyan |
sa yaH sa pApmA yad evedam apratirUpaM jighrati |
sa eva sa pApmA || BrhUp_1,3.3 ||>#


#<atha ha cakShur Ucus tvaM na udgAyeti |
tatheti tebhyash cakShur udagAyat |
yash cakShuShi bhogas taM devebhya AgAyat |
yat kalyANaM pashyati tad Atmane |
te 'vidur anena vai na udgAtrAtyeShyantIti |
tam abhidrutya pApmanAvidhyan |
sa yaH sa pApmA yad evedam apratirUpaM pashyati |
sa eva sa pApmA || BrhUp_1,3.4 ||>#


#<atha ha shrotram Ucus tvaM na udgAyeti |
tatheti tebhyaH shrotram udagAyat |
yaH shrotre bhogas taM devebhya AgAyat |
yat kalyANaM shR^iNoti tad Atmane |
te 'vidur anena vai na udgAtrAtyeShyantIti |
tam abhidrutya pApmanAvidhyan |
sa yaH sa pApmA |
yad evedam apratirUpaM shR^iNoti |
sa eva sa pApmA || BrhUp_1,3.5 ||>#


#<atha ha mana Ucus tvaM na udgAyeti |
tatheti tebhyo mana udagAyat |
yo manasi bhogas taM devebhya AgAyat |
yat kalyANaM saMkalpayati tad Atmane |
te 'vidur anena vai na udgAtrAtyeShyantIti |
tam abhidrutya pApmanAvidhyan |
sa yaH sa pApmA |
yad evedam apratirUpaM saMkalpayati |
sa eva sa pApmA |
evam u khalv etA devatAH pApmabhir upAsR^ijan |
evam enAH pApmanAvidhyan || BrhUp_1,3.6 ||>#

__________

BrhUpBh_1,3.3-6 tathaiva ghrANAdidevatA udgIthanirvartatvAjjapamantraprakAshyA upAsyAshceti kameNa parIkShitavantaH /
devAnAM caitannishcitamAsIt- vAgAdidevatAH kameNa parIkShyamANAH kalyANaviShayavisheShAtmasambandhAsaN^gahetorAsurapApmasaMsargAd udgIthanirvartanAsamarthAH /
ato 'nabhidheyAH"asato mA sadgamaya"ityanupAsyAshca, ashuddhatvAditarAvyApakatvAcceti /
evamu khalvanuktA apyetAstvagAdidevatAH kalyANAkalyANAkAryadarshanAdevaM vAgAdideva, enAH pApmanAvidhyanpApmanA viddhavanta iti yaduktaM tatpApmabhirupAsR^ijanpApmabhiH saMsargaM kR^itavanta ityetat //3-6 //


vAgAdidevatA upAsInA api mR^ityatigamanAyAsharaNAH santo devAH krameNa-

START BrhUp 1,3.7

#<atha hemam AsanyaM prANam Ucus tvaM na udgAyeti |
tatheti tebhya eSha prANa udagAyat |
te 'vidur anena vai na udgAtrAtyeShyantIti |
tam abhidrutya pApmanAvivyatsan |
sa yathAshmAnam R^itvA loShTo vidhvaMsetaivaM haiva vidhvaMsamAnA viShvaJNco vineshuH |
tato devA abhavan, parAsurA |
bhavaty AtmanA, parAsya dviShan bhrAtR^ivyo bhavati ya evaM veda || BrhUp_1,3.7 ||>#

__________

BrhUpBh_1,3.7 athAnantaraM ha imamityabhinayapradarshanArtham /
AsanyamAsye bhavamAsanyaM mukhAntarbilasthaM prANamUcustvaM na udgAyeti /
tathetyevaM sharaNamupagatebhyaH sa eSha prANo mukhya udagAyadityAdi pUrvavat /
pApmanAvivyatsanvedhanaM kartumiShTavantaste ca doShAsaMsargiNaM santaM mukhyaM prANam /
svena AsaN^gadoSheNa vAgAdiShu labdhaprasarAstadabhyAsAnuvR^ittyA saMsrakShyamANA vineshurvinaShTA vidhvastAH /
kathamiva? iti dR^iShTAnta ucyate- sa yathA sa dR^iShTAnto yathA loke 'shmAnaM pAShANamR^itvA gatvA prApya, loShTaH pAMsupiNDaH pAShANacUrNanAyAshmani nikShiptaH svayaM vidhvaMseta vistraMseta vicUrNIbhavet, evaM haiva yathAyaM dR^iShTAnta evameva, vidhvaMsamAnA visheSheNa dhvaMsamAnA viShvaJNco nAnAgatayo vineshurvinaShTA yataH, tatastasmAdAsuravinAshAddevatvapratibandhabhUtebhyaH svAbhAvikAsaN^gajanitapApmabhyo viyogAd asaMsargadharmimukhyaprANAshrayabalAd devA vAgAdayaH prakR^itA abhavat /
kimabhavan? svaM devatArUpamagnyAdyAtmakaM vakShyamANam /
pUrvamaShyagnyAdyAtmana eva santaH svAbhAvikena pApmanA tiraskR^itavij~nAnAH piNDamAtrAbhimAnA Asan /
te tatpApmaviyogAdujjhitvA piNDamAtrAbhimAnaM shAstrasamarpitavAgAdyagnyAdyAtmAbhimAnA babhUvurityarthaH /
kiJNca te pratipakShabhUtA asurAH parAbhavannityanuvartate /
parAbhUtA vinaShTA ityarthaH /
yathA purAkalpena varNitaH pUrvayajamAno 'tikrAntakAlikaH etAmevAkhyAyikArUpAM shrutiM dR^iShTvA tenaiva krameNa vAgAdidevatAH parIkShya, tAshcApohyAsaN^gapApmAspadadoShavattvenAdoShAspadaM mukhyaM prANamAtmatvenopagamya vAgAdyAdhyAtmikapiNDamAtraparicchinnAtmAbhimAnaM hitvA vairAjapiNDAbhimAnaM vAgAdyagnyAdyAtmaviShayaM vartamAnaprajApatitvaM shAstraprakAshitaM pratipannaH, tathaivAyaM yajamAnastenaiva vidhinA bhavati prajApatisvarUpeNAtmanA /
parA cAsyA prajApatitvapratipakShabhUtaH pApmA dviShanbhrAtR^ivyo bhavati /
yato 'dveShTApi bhavati kashcid bhrAtR^ivyo bharatAditulyaH, yastvindriyaviShayAsaN^gajanitaH pApmA bhrAtR^ivyo dveShTA ca, pAramArthikAtmasvarUpatiratiraskaraNahetutvAt sa ca parAbhavati vishIryate loShTavAtprANapariShvaN^gAt /
kasyaitatphalam? ityAha- ya evaM veda /
yathoktaM prANamAtmatvena pratipadyate pUrvayajamAnavadityarthaH //7//



phalamupasaMhR^ityAdhunAkhyAyikArUpamevAshrityAha- kasmAccahetorvAgAdInmuktA mukhya eva prANa AtmatvenAshrayitavyaH? iti tadupapattinirUpaNAya yasmAdayaM vAgAdInAM piNDAdInAM ca sAdhAraNa AtmA, ityetamarthamAkhyAyikayA darshayantyAha shrutiH-

START BrhUp 1,3.8

#<te hocuH -- kva nu so 'bhUd yo na ittham asakteti |
ayam Asye 'ntar iti |
so 'yAsya AN^giraso 'N^gAnAM hi rasaH || BrhUp_1,3.8 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_1,3.8 te prajApatiprANA mukhyena prANena pariprApitadevasvarUpA hocuruktavantaH phalAvasthAH /
kim? ityAha- kva nviti vitarke /
kva nu kasminnu so 'bhUt /
kaH? yo no 'smAnitthamevamasakta saJNjitavAndevabhAvamAtmatvenopagamitavAn /
smaranti hi loke kenacidupakR^itA upakAriNam /
lokavadeva smaranto vicArayamANAH kAryakaraNasaMghAte AtmanyevopalabdhavantaH /
katham? ayamAsye 'ntariti, Asye mukhe ya AkAshastasminnantarayaM pratyakSho vartata iti /
sarvo hi loko vicAryAdhyavasyati, tathA devAH /
yasmAdayamantarAkAshe vAgAdyAtmatvena visheShamanAshritya vartamAna upalabdho devaiH, tasmAtsaprANo 'yAsyo visheShAnAshrayAcca asakta saJNjitavAnvAgAdIn /
ata evAN^girasa AtmA kAryakaraNAnAm /
kathamAN^girasaH? prasiddhaM hyetadaN^gAnAM kAryakaraNalakShaNAnAM rasaH sAra AtmetyarthaH /
kathaM punaraN^garasatvam? tadapAye shoShaprApteriti vakShyAmaH /
yasmAccAyamaN^garasatvAdvisheShAmAshritatvAcca kAryakaraNAnAM sAdhAraNa AtmA vishuddhashca, tasmAdvAgAdInapAsya prANa evAtmatvenAshrayitavya iti vAkyArthaH /
AtmA hyAtmatvenopagantavyo 'viparItabodhAcchreyaHprApteH, viparyaye svAniShTaprAptidarshanAt //8//



syAnmataM prANasya vishuddhirasiddheti /
nanu parihR^itametadvAgAdInAM kalyANavadanAdyAsaN^gavatprANasya AsaN^gAspadatvAbhAvena /
vADham, kiM tvAN^girasatvena vAgAdInAmAtmatvoktyA vAgAdidvAreNa shavasR^iShTitatspR^iShTerivAshuddhatA shaN^kyate- ityAha- shuddha eva praNaH /
kutaH?

START BrhUp 1,3.9

#<sA vA eShA devatA dUr nAma |
dUraM hy asyA mR^ityur |
dUraM ha vA asmAn mR^ityur bhavati ya evaM veda || BrhUp_1,3.9 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_1,3.9 sA vA eShA devatA dUrnAma /
yaM prANaM prApyAshmAnamiva loShTavadvidhvastA asurAstaM parAmR^ishati seti /
saivaiShA yeyaM vartamAnayajamAnasharIrasthA devairnirdhAritA"ayamAsye 'ntaH"iti /
devatA ca sA syAt, upAsanakriyAyAH karmabhAvena guNabhUtatvAt /
yasyAtmA dUrnAma dUrityevaM khyAtA /
nAmashabdaH khyApanaparyAyaH /
tasmAtprasiddhAsyA vishuddhidUrnAmatvAt /
kutaH punardUrnAmatvam? ityAha- dUraM dUreH hi yasmAdasyAH prANadevatAyAH mR^ityurAsaN^galakShaNaH pApmA /
asaMshleShadharmitvAtprANasya samIpasthAsyApi dUratA mR^ityostasmAd dUrityevaM khyAtiH, evaM prANasya vishuddhirj~nApitA /
viduShaH phalamucyate- dUraM ha vA asmAnmR^ityurbhavati /
asmAdevaMvidaH, ya evaM veda tasmAdevamiti prakR^itaM vishuddhiguNopetaM prANamupAsta ityarthaH /
upAsanaM nAma upAsyArthavAde yathA devatAdisvarUpaM shrutyA j~nApyate tathA manasopagamya AsanaM cintanaM laukikapratyayAvyavadhAnena yAvattaddevatAdisvarUpAtmAbhimAnAbhivyaktiriti laukikAtmAbhimAnavat /
"devo bhUtvA devAnapyeti" (bR^i.u.4 / 1 / 2) "kindevato 'syAM prAcyAM dishyasi" (bR^i.u.3 / 9 / 20) ityevamAdishrutibhyaH //9//



sA vA eShA devatA dUraM ha vA asmAnmR^ityurbhavatItyuktam /
kathaM punarevaMvido dUraM mR^ityurbhavati? ityucyate- evaMvittvavirodhAt /
indriyaviShayasaMsargAsaN^gajo hi pApmA prANAtmAbhimAnino hi virudhyate, vAgAdivisheShAtmAbhimAnahetutvAt svAbhAvikAj~nAnahetutvAcca /
shAstrajanito hi prANAtmAbhimAnaH /
tasmAdevaMvidaH pApmA dUraM bhavatIti yuktaM virodhAt /
tadetatpradarshayati-

START BrhUp 1,3.10

#<sA vA eShA devataitAsAM devatAnAM pApmAnaM mR^ityum apahatya yatrAsAM dishAm antas tad gamayAM cakAra |
tad AsAM pApmano vinyadadhAt |
tasmAn na janam iyAn nAntam iyAn net pApmAnaM mR^ityum anvavAyAnIti || BrhUp_1,3.10 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_1,3.10 sA vA eShA devatetyuktArtham /
etAsAM vAgAdInAM devatAnAM pApmAnaM mR^ityuM svAbhAvikAj~nAnaprayuktendriyaviShayasaMsargAsaN^gajanitena hi pApmanA sarvo mriyate, sa hyato mR^ityuH, taM prANAtmAbhimAnamAtratayaiva prANo 'pahantetyucyate /
virodhAdeva tu pApmaivaMvido dUraM gato bhavati /
kiM punashcakAra devatAnAM pApmAnaM mR^ityumapahatya? ityucyate- yatra yasminnAsAM prAcyAdInAM dishAmanto 'vasAnaM tattatra gamayAJNcakAra gamanaM kR^itavAnityetat /
nanu nAsti dishAmantaH kathamantaM gamitavAn? ityucyate- shrautavij~nAnavajjanAvadhinimittakalpitatvAddishAM tadvirodhijanAvyuShita eva desho dishAmantaH, deshAnto 'raNyamiti yadvadityadoShaH /
tattatra gamayitvA AsAM devatAnAm, pApmana iti dvitIyAbahuvacanam, vinyadadhAdvividhaM nyagbhAvenadadhAtsthApitavatI prANadevatA /
prANAtmAbhimAnashUnyeShu antyajaneShviti sAmarthyAt /
indriyasaMsargajo hi sa iti prANyAshrayatAvagamyate /
tasmAttamantyaM janaM neyAnna gacchetsambhAShaNadarshanAdibhirna saMsR^ijet /
tatsaMsarge pApmanA saMsargaH kR^itaH syAtpApmAshrayo hi saH /
tajjananivAsaM cAntaM digantashabdavAcyaM neyAjjanashUnyamapi, janamapi taddeshaviyuktamityabhiprAyaH /
nediti paribhayArthe nipAtaH /
itthaM janasaMsarge pApmAnaM mR^ityumanvavAyAnIti /
anu ava ayAnItyanugaccheyamiti, evaM bhIto na janamantaM ceyAditi pUrveNa sambandhaH //10//

START BrhUp 1,3.11

#<sA vA eShA devataitAsAM devatAnAM pApmAnaM mR^ityum apahatyAthainA mR^ityum atyavahat || BrhUp_1,3.11 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_1,3.11 sA vA eShA devatA, tadetatprANAtmaj~nAnakarmaphalaM vAgAdInAmagnyAdyAtmatvamucyate /
athainA mR^ityumatyavahat tasmAdAdhyAtmikaparicchedakaraH pApmA mR^ityuH prANAtmavij~nAnenapahatastasmAtsaprANo 'pahantA pApmano mR^ityoH /
tasmAtsa eva prANa enA vAgAdidevatAH prakR^itaM pApmAnaM mR^ityumatItya avahatprApayatsvaM svamaparicchinnamagnyAdidevAtAtmarUpam //11//

START BrhUp 1,3.12

#<sA vai vAcam eva prathamAm atyavahat |
sA yadA mR^ityum atyamucyata so 'gnir abhavat |
so 'yam agniH pareNa mR^ityum atikrAnto dIpyate || BrhUp_1,3.12 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_1,3.12. sa vai vAcameva prathamAmatyavahat /
sa prANo vAcameva prathamAM pradhAnAmityetat /
udgIthakarmaNItarakaraNApekShayA sAdhakatamatvaM prAdhAnyaM tasyAH /
tAM prathamAmatyavahadvahanaM kR^itavAn /
tasyAH punarmR^ityumatItyoDhAyAH kiM rUpam? ityucyate- sA vAgyadA yasminkAle pApmAnaM mR^ityum atyamucyatAtItyAmucyata mocitA svayameva, tadAsognirabhavat /
sA vAkpUrvamapyagnireva satI mR^ityuviyoge 'pyagnirevAbhavat /
etAvAMstu visheSho mR^ityuviyoge /
soyamatikrAnto 'gniH pareNamR^ityuM parastAnmR^ityordIpyate /
prAÇmokShAnmR^ityupratibaddho adhyAtmavAgAtmanA nedAnImiva dIptimAnAsIt, idAnIM tu mR^ityuM pareNa dIpyate mR^ityuviyogAt //12//

START BrhUp 1,3.13

#<atha prANam atyavahat |

START BrhUp 1,3.16

#<atha mano 'tyavahat |
tad yadA mR^ityum atyamucyata sa candramA abhavat |
so 'sau candraH pareNa mR^ityum atikrAnto bhAti |
evaM ha vA enam eShA devatA mR^ityum ativahati ya evaM veda || BrhUp_1,3.16 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_1,3.16 manashcandramA bhAti /
yathA pUrvayajamAnaM vAgAdyagnyAdibhAvena mR^ityumatyavahat, evamenaM vartamAnayajamAnamapi ha vA eShA prANadevatA mR^ityumativahati vAgAdyagnyAdibhAvena /
evaM yo vAgAdipaJNcakavishiShTaM prANaM veda /
"taM yathA yathopAsate tadeva bhavati"iti shruteH //16//

START BrhUp 1,3.17

#<athAtmane 'nnAdyam AgAyat |
yad dhi kiJNcAnnam adyate 'nenaiva tad adyate |
iha pratitiShThati || BrhUp_1,3.17 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_1,3.17 yathA vAgAdibhirAtmArthamAgAnaM kR^itaM tathA mukhyo 'pi prANaH sarvaprANasAdhAraNaM prAjApatyaphalamAgAnaM kR^itvA triShu pamAneShu, athAnantaraM shiShTeShu navasu, stotreShu, Atmane AtmArthamannAdyamannaM ca tadAdyaM cAnnAdyamAgAyat /
kartuH kAmasaMyogo vAcanika ityuktam /
kathaM punastadannAdyaM prANenAtmArthamAgItamiti gamyate? ityatra hetumAha- yatkiJNceti sAmAnyAnnamAtraparAmarshArthaH /
hIti hetau /
yasmAlloke prANibhiryadkiJNcidannamadyatebhakShyate tadanenaiva /
ana iti prANasyAkhyA prasiddhA anaH shabdaH sAntaH shakaTavAcI, yastvanyaH svarAntaH sa prANaparyAyaH /
prANenaiva tadadyata ityarthaH /
kiJNca na kevalaM prANenAdyata evAnnAdyam, tasmiJNcharIrAkArapariNate 'nnAdya iha pratitiShThati prANaH /
tasmAtprANenAtmanaH pratiShThArthamAgItamannAdyam /
yadapi prANenAnnAdanaM tadapi pratiShThArthameveti na vAgAdiShviva kalyANasaN^gajapAtmasambhavaH prANe 'sti //17//



nanvavadhAraNamayuktaM prANenaiva tadadyata iti, vAgAdInAmapi annanimittopakAradarshanAt /

START BrhUp 1,3.18

#<te devA abruvan |

BrhUpBh_1,3.18 te vAgAdayo devAH, svaviShayadyotanAddevAH, abruvannuktavanto mukhyaM prANam idametAvannAto 'dhikamasti /

vAgAdyAshrayaM prANaM yo veda vAgAdayashca paJNca prANAshrayA iti tamapyevamevaM ha vai svA j~nAtasya abhisaMvishanti vAgAdaya iva prANam /
j~nAtInAmAshrayaNIyo bhavatItyabhiprAyaH /
abhisanniviShTAnAM ca svAnAM prANavadeva vAgAdInAM svAnnena bhartA bhavati /
tathA shreShThaH puro 'grata etA gantA bhavati vAgAdInAmiva prANaH /
tathAnnAdo 'nAmayAvItyarthaH /
adhipatiradhiShThAya ca pAlayitA svatantraH patiH prANavadeva vAgAdInAm /
ya evaM prANaM veda tasyaitadyathoktaM phalaM bhavati /
kiJNca ya u haivaMvidhaM prANavidaM prati sveShu j~nAtInAM madhye pratiH pratikUlo bubhUrShati pratispardhI bhavitumicchati, sosurA iva, prANapratispardhino na haivAlaM na paryApto bhAryebhyo bharaNIyebhyo bhavati bhartumityarthaH /
atha punarya evaM j~nAtInAM madhye evaMvidaM vAgAdaya iva prANam anu anugato bhavati, yo vaitamevaMvidamanvevAnuvartayanneva AtmIyAnbhAryAn bubhUrShati bhartumicchati, yathaiva vAgAdayaH prANAnuvR^ittyAtmabubhUrShava Asan /
sa haivAlaM paryApto bhAryebhyo bharaNIyebhyo bhavati bhartuM netaraH svatantraH /
sarvametatprANaguNavij~nAnaphalamuktam //18//



kAryakaraNAnAmAtmatvapratipAdanAya prANasyAN^girasatvamupanyastaM so 'yAsya AN^girasa iti /

START BrhUp 1,3.19

#<so 'yAsya AN^giraso 'N^gAnAM hi rasaH |

BrhUpBh_1,3.19 so 'yAsya AN^girasa ityAdi yathopanyastamevopAdIyate uttarArtham'prANo vA aN^gAnAM rasaH'ityevamantaM vAkyaM yathAvyAkhyArthameva punaH smArayati /

START BrhUp 1,3.21

BrhUpBh_1,3.21 eSha u eva brahmaNaspatiH /

START BrhUp 1,3.22 

#<eSha u eva sAma |

START BrhUp 1,3.28

#<athAtaH pavamAnAnAm evAbhyArohaH |
sa vai khalu prastotA sAma prastauti |

asato mA sad gamaya, tamaso mA jyotir gamaya, mR^ityor mAmR^itaM gamayeti |

BrhUpBh_1,3.28 athAnantaraM yasmAccaivaM viduShA prayujyamAnaM devabhAvAyAbhyArohaphalaM japakarma, atastasmAttadvidhIyata iha /

tatra vAkyArthamAha- amR^itaM mA kurvityevaitadAheti /
tathA tamaso mA jyotirgamayeti mR^ityurgamayeti /
mR^ityurvai tamaH sarvaM hyaj~nAnamAvaraNAtmakatvAttamaH tadeva ca maraNahetutvAnmR^ityuH /
jyotiramR^itaM pUrvoktaviparItaM daivaM svarUpam /
prakAshAtmakatvAjj~nAnaM jyotiH, tadevAmR^itamavinAshAtmakatvAt /
tasmAt tamaso mA jyotirgamayeti pUrvavanmR^ityormAmR^itaM gamayetyAdi /
amR^itaM mA kurvityevaitadAha- daivaM prAjApatyaM phalabhAvamApAdayetyarthaH /
pUrvo mantro 'sAdhanasvabhAvAt sAdhanabhAvamApAdayeti /
dvitIyastu sAdhanabhAvAdapi aj~nAnarUpAt sAdhyabhAvamApAdayeti /
mR^ityormAmR^itaM gamayeti pUrvayoreva mantrayoH samucitor'thastR^itIyena mantreNocyata iti prasiddhArthataiva /
nAtra tR^itIye mantre tirohitamantarhitamivArtharUpaM pUrvayoriva mantrayorasti, yathAshruta evArthaH /
yAjamAnamudgAnaM kR^itvA pavamAneShu triShu, athAnantaraM yAnItarANi shiShTAni stotrANi teShvAtmane 'nnAdyamAgAyet prANavidudgAtAprANabhUtaH prANavadeva /
yasmAtsa eva udgAtaivaM prANaM yathoktaM vetti, ataH prANavadeva taM kAmaM sAdhayituM samarthaH /
tasmAdyajamAnasteShu stotreShu prayujyamAneShu varaM vR^iNIta, yaM kAmaM kAmayeta taM kAmaM varaM vR^iNIta prArthayeta /
yasmAtsa eSha evaMvidudgAteti tasmAcchabdAtprAgeva sambadhyate /
Atmane vA yajamAnAya vA yaM kAmaM kAmayate icchatyudgAtA tamAgAyatyAgAnena sAdhayati /
evaM tAvajj~nAnakarmabhyAM prANAtmApattirityuktam /
tatra nAstyAshaN^kAsambhavaH /
ataH karmApAye prANApattirbhavati vA na vA? ityAshaN^kate /
tadAshaN^kAnivR^ittyarthamAha- taddhaitalokajideveti /
taddhatadetatprANadarshanaM karmaviyuktaM kevalamapi, lokajideveti lokasAdhanameva /
na ha evAlokyatAyai alokArhatvAya AshA AshaMsanaM prArthanaM naivAsti ha /
na hi prANAtmani utpannAtmAbhimAnasya tatprAptyAshaMsanaM sambhavati /
na hi grAmasthaH kadA grAmaM prApnutAmityaraNyastha ivAshAste /
asannikR^iShTaviShaye hyanAtmanyAshaMsanam, na tatsvAtmani sambhavati /
tasmAnnAshAsti kadAcitprANAtmabhAvaM na prapadyeyamiti /
kasyaitat? ya evametatsAma prANaM yathoktaM nirdhAritamahimAnaM veda- ahamasmi prANa indriyaviShayAsaN^gairAsuraiH pApmabhiradharShaNIyo vishuddhaH, vAgAdipaJNcakaM ca madAshrayatvAdagnyAdyAtmarUpaM svAbhAvikavij~nAnotthendriyaviShayAsaN^gajanitAsurapApmadoShaviyuktaM sarvabhUteShu ca madAshrayAnnAdyopayogabandhanam, AtmA cAhaM sarvabhUtAnAmAN^girasatvAt, R^igyajuH sAmodgIthabhUtAyAshca vAca AtmA tadvayAptestannirvartakatvAcca, mama sAmno gItibhAvamApadyamAnasya bAhyaM dhanaM bhUShaNaM sausvaryaM tato 'pyAntaraM sauvarNyalAkShaNikaM sausvaryam, gItibhAvamApadyamAnasya mama kaNThAdisthAnAni pratiShThA /
evaM guNo 'haM puttikAdisharIreShu kArtsnyena parisamApto 'mUrtatvAtsarvagatatvAcca- iti A evamabhimAnAbhivyaktervedopAsta ityarthaH //28//

#<iti prathamAdhyAye tR^itIyamudgIthabrAhmaNam //3//>#



j~nAnakarmabhyAM samucitAbhyAM prajApatitvaprAptirvyAkhyAtA kevalaprANadarshanena ca'taddhaitallokajideva'ityAdinA /
prajApateH phalabhUtasya sR^iShTisthitisaMhAreShu jagataH svAtantryAdivibhUtyupavarNanena j~nAnakarmaNorvaidikayoH phalotkarSho varNayitavya ityevamarthamArabhyate /
tena ca karmakANDavihitaj~nAnakarmastutiH kR^itvA bhavetsAmarthyAt /
vivakShitaM tvetat- sarvamapyetajj~nAnakarmaphalaM saMsAra eva, bhayAratyAdiyuktatvashravaNAt, kAryakaraNalakShaNatvAcca sthUlavyaktAnityaviShayatvAcceti /
brahmavidyAyAH kevalAyA vakShyamANAyA mokShahetutvamityuttarArthaM ceti /
na hi saMsAraviShayAtsAdhyasAdhanAdibhedalakShaNAd aviraktasya Atmaikatva j~nAnaviShaye 'dhikAraH, atR^iShitasyeva pAne /
tasmAjj~nAnakarmaphalotkarShopavarNanamuttarArtham /
tathA ca vakShyati-"tadetatpadanIyamasya"(bR^i.u.1 / 4 / 7) "tadetatpreyaH putrAt" (bR^i.u.1 / 4 / 8) ityAdi /

START BrhUp 1,4.1

#<Atmaivedam agra AsIt puruShavidhaH |

BrhUpBh_1,4.6 evaM sa prajApatirjagadidaM mithunAtmakaM sR^iShTA brahmaNAdivarNaniyanvardevatAH sisR^ikShurAdau, ayeti shabdadvayamabhinayapradarshanArtham, anena prakAreNa mukhe hastau prakShityAbhyamanyadAbhimukhyena manyanapakarot /

yasmAddAhakasyAgneryoniretadubhayaM hastau mukhaM ca, tasmAdbhaya mapyetadalomakaM lomavivarjitam /
kiM sarvameva? na, antarato 'bhyantarataH;asti hi yonyA sAmAnyamubhayasyAsya /
kim? alomakA hi yonirantarataH strINAm /
tathA brAhmaNo 'pi mukhAdeva jajhe prajApateH /
tasmAdekayonitvAjjayeShThenevAnujo 'nugR^ihyate agninA brAhmaNaH /
tasmAdbrAhmaNo 'gnidevatyo mukhavIryashceti shrutismR^itisiddham /
tathA balAshrayAbhyAM bAhubhyAM balabhidAdikaM kShanniyajAtiniyantarAM kShanniyaM ca /
tasmAdaindraM kShatraM bAhuvIryaM ceti shrutau smR^itau cAvagatam /
tathoruta IhA ceShTA tadAshrayAdvasvAdilakShaNaM visho niyantAraM vishaM ca /
tasmAtkR^iShyAdiparo vasvAdidevatyashca vaishyaH /
tathA pUShaNaM pR^ithvIdaivataM shUdraM ca padbhyAM paricaraNakShamamasR^ijateti shrutismR^itiprasiddheH /
tatra kShatrAdidevatAsargamihAnuktaM vakShyamANamamapyuktavadupasaMharati sR^iShTisAkalyAnukIrtyai /
yatheyaM shrutirvyavasthitA tathA prajApatireva sarve devA iti nishcitor'thaH /
sraShTurananyatvAtsR^iShTAnAm /
prajApatinaiva tu sR^iShTatvAd devAnAm /
athaivaM prakaraNArthe vyavasthite tatstutyabhiprAyeNAvidvanmatAntaranindopanyAsaH, anyanindAnyastutaye /
tattatra karmaprakaraNe kevalayAj~nikA yAgakAle yadidaM vaca AhuH -'amumagniM yajAsumindraM yaja'ityAdi - nAmashastrastotrakarmAdibhinnatvAdbhinnamevAgnyAdidevamevaikaM manyamAnA AhurityabhiprAyaH /
tanna tathA vidyAt, yasmAdetasyaiva prajApateH sA visR^iShTirdevabhedaH sarva eSha u hyeva prajApatireva prANaH sarve devAH /
atra vipratipadyante - para eva hiraNyagarbhe ityeke /
saMsArItyapare /
paraM eva tu mantravarNAt /
"indraM mitraM varuNamagnimAhuH"iti shruteH /
"eSha brahmaiSha indra eSha prajApatirete sarve devAH"(ai.u.5 / 3) iti ca shruteH /
smR^iteshca -"etameke vadantyagniM manumanye prajApatim"(manu.12 / 123) iti"yo 'sAvatIndriyo 'grAhyaH sUkShmo 'vyaktaH sanAtanaH /
sarvabhUtamayo 'cintyaH sa eva svayamudbabhau" /
(manu.1 / 7) iti /
saMsAryeva vA syAt /
"sarvainpApmana aupat"(bR^i.u.1 / 4 / 1) iti shruteH /
na hyasaMsAriNaH pApmadAhaprasaN^go 'sti /
bhayAratisaMyogashravaNAt /
"atha yanmartyaH sannamR^itAnasR^ijata"(bR^i.u.1 / 4 / 6) iti ca /
"hiraNyagarbhaM pashyati jAyamAnam"(shve.u.4 / 12) iti ca mantravarNAt /
smR^iteshca karmavipAkaprakriyAyAm -"brahmA vishvasR^ijo dharmo mahAnavyaktameva ca /
uttamAM sAtvikImetAM gatimAhurmanIShiNaH"(manu.12 / 50) iti /
athaivaM viruddhArthAnupapatteH prAmANyavyAghAta iti cet? na, kalpanAntaropapatteravirodhAt /
upAdhivisheShasambandhAdvisheShakalpanAntaramupapadyate /
"AsIno dUraM vrajati shayAno yAti sarvataH /
kastaM madAmadaM devaM madanyo j~nAtumarhati"(ka.u.1 / 2 / 21) ityevamAdishrutibhya upAdhivashAtsaMsAritvaM na paramArthataH /
svato 'saMsAryeva /
evamekatvaM nAnAtvaM ca hiraNyagarbhasya /
tathA sarvajIvAnAm, tattvamasi (chA.u.6 / 8 -16) iti shruteH /
hiraNyagarbhastu upAdhishuddhyatishayApekShayA prAyashaH para eveti shrutismR^itivAdAH pravR^ittAH /
saMsAritvaM tu kvacideva darshayanti /
jIvAnAM upAdhigatAshuddhibAhulyAtsaMsAritvameva prAyasho 'bhilapyate /
vyAvR^ittakR^itsnopAdhibhedApekShayA tu sarvaH paratvenAbhidhIyate shrutismR^itivAdaiH /
tArkikaistu parityaktAgamabalairasti nAsti kartAkartetyAdi viruddhaM bahu tarkapadbhirAkulIkR^itaH shAstrArthaH, tenArthanishcayo durlabhaH /
ye tu kevalashAstrAnusAriNaH shAntadarpAsteShAM pratyakShaviShaya iva nishcitaH shAstrArthe devatAdiviShayaH /
tatra prajApaterekasya devasyAtrAdyalakShaNo bhedo vivakShita iti tatrAgnirukto 'ttA, AdyaH soma idAnImucyate - atha yatkiJNcedaM loka ArdraM dravAtmakaM tadretasa AtmAno bIjAdasR^ijata;retasa ApaH (ai.u.1 / 4) iti shruteH /
dravAtmakashca somaH /
tasmAdyadArdraM prajApatinA retasaH sR^iShTaM tadu soma eva /
etAvadvai etAvadeva nAto 'dhikamidaM sarvam /
kiM tat? annaM caiva somo dravAtmakatvAdApyAyakam /
annAdashcAgnirauShNyAd rUkShatvAcca /
tatraivadhriyate, soma evAnnaM yadadyate tadeva soma ityarthaH /
ya evAttA sa evAgniH arthabalAddhyavadhAraNam /
agnirapi kvacid hUyamAnaH somapakShasyaiva /
somo 'pIjyamAno 'gnirevAttR^itvAt /
evamagnIShomAtmakaM jagadAtmatvena pashyanta kenaciddoSheNa lipyate, prajApatishca bhavati /
saiShA brahmaNaH prajApateratisR^iShTirAtmano 'pyatishayA /
kA sA ityAha - yacchreyasaH prashasyatarAnAtmanaH sakAshAdyasmAdasR^ijata devAMstasmAddevasR^iShTiratisR^iShTiH /
kathaM punarAtmano 'tishayA sR^iShTiH ityata Aha - atha yadyasmAnmartyaH sanmaraNadharmA sannamR^itAnamaraNadharmiNo devAn karmaj~nAnavahninA sarvAnAtmanaH pApmana oShitvAsR^ijata, tasmAdetAmatisR^iShTiM prajApaterAtmabhUtAM yo veda sa etasyAmatisR^iShTyAM prajApatiriva bhavati prajApativadeva sraShTA bhavati //6//


sarvaM vaidikaM sAdhanaM j~nAnakarmalakShaNaM kartrAdyanekakArakApekShaM prajApatitvaphalAvasAnaM sAdhyametAvadeva yadetadvyAkR^itaM jagatsaMsAraH /
athaitasyaiva sAdhyasAdhanalakShaNasya vyAkR^itasya jagato vyAkaraNAtprAgbIjAvasthA yA tAM nirdidij~natyaN^kurAdikAryAnumitAmiva vR^ikShasya, karmabIjo 'vidyAkShetro hyasau saMsAravR^ikShaH samUla uddhartavya iti /

BrhUpBh_1,4.7 tadvedaM taditi bIjAvasthaM jagatprAgutpattestarhi tasminkAle;parokShatvAsarvanAmnApratyakShAbhidhAnenAbhidhIyate, bhUtakAlasambandhitvAdavyAkR^itabhAvino jagataH;sukhagrahaNArthamaitihyaprayogo ha shabdaH /

yathedaM jaganniyantrAdyanekakArakanimittAdivisheShavadvyAkR^itam, tathA aparityaktAnyatamavisheShavadeva tadavyAkR^itam /
vyAkR^itAvyAkR^itamAtraM tu visheShaH /
dR^iShTashca loke vivakShAtaH shabdaprayogo grAma Agato grAmaH shUnya iti /
kadAcid grAmashabdena nivAsamAtravivakShAyAM grAmaH shUnya iti shabdaprayogo bhavati, kadAcinnivAsijanavivakShAyAM grAma Agata iti, kadAcidubhayavivakShAyAmapi grAmashabdaprayogo bhavati, grAmaM ca na pravishediti yathA /
tadvadihApi jagadidaM vyAkR^itamavyAkR^itaM cetyabhedavivakShAyAm AtmAnAtmanorbhavati vyapadeshaH /

tathA mahAnaja AtmA (bR^i.u.4 / 4 / 22) asthUlo 'naNuH sa eSha neti neti (bR^i.u.3 / 9 / 26) ityAdi kevalAtmavyapadeshaH /

nAkAshena kiJNcinnityapraviShTatvAt /

START BrhUp 1,4.8

#<tad etat preyaH putrAt preyo vittAt preyo 'nyasmAt sarvasmAd antarataraM yad ayam AtmA |

BrhUpBh_1,4.8 tadetadAtmatattvaM preyaH priyataraM putrAt /
putro hi loke priyaH prasiddhastasmAdapi priyataramiti niratishayapriyatvaM darshayati /
tathA vittAddhiraNyaratnAdeH, tathA anyasyAdyalloke priyatvena prasiddhaM tasmAtsarvasmAdityarthaH /
tatkasmAdAtmatattvameva priyataraM na prANAdi? ityucyate - antarataraM bAhyAtputravittAdeH prANapiNDasamudAyo hyantaro 'bhyantaraH sannikR^iShTa AtmanaH /
tasmAdapyantarAdantarataraM yadayamAtmA yadetadAtmatattvam /

tathAyamAtmA sarvalaukikapriyebhyaH priyatamaH /

kim? priyaM tavAbhimataM putrAdilakShaNaM rotsyatyAvaraNaM prANasaMrodhaM prApsyati /
vinaN^kShyatIti /
sa kasmAdevaM bravIti? yasmAdIshvaraH samarthaH paryApto 'sAvevaM vaktuM ha yasmAttasmAttathaiva syAdyattenoktaM prANasaMrodhaM prApsyati /
yathAbhUtavAdI hi saH, tasmAtsa Ishvaro vaktum /
IshvarashabdaH kShipravAcIti kecit /
bhavedyadi prasiddhiH syAt /
tasmAdujjhitvAnyatpriyamAtmAnameva priyamupAsIta /
sa ya AtmAnameva priyamupAste, Atmaiva priyo nAnyo 'stIti pratipadyate 'nyallaukikaM priyamapyapriyameveti nishcitya upAste cintayati, na hAsyaivaMvidaH priyaM pramAyukaM pramaraNashIlaM bhavati /
nityAnuvAdamAtrametat, Atmavido 'nyasya priyasyApriyasya cAbhAvAt /
AtmapriyagrahaNastutyarthaM vA priyaguNaphalavidhAnArthaM mandAtmadarshinaH /
tAcchIlyapratyayopAdAnAt //8//

BrhUpBh_1,4.9 taditi vakShyamANamanantaravAkye 'vadyotyaM vastvAhuH /

BrhUpBh_1,4.10 brahmAparam, sarvabhAvasya sAdhyatvopapatteH /

tayAvipariluptayA nityayA dR^iShTyA svarUpabhUtayA svayaJNjyotiHsamAkhyathetAmanityAM dR^iShTiM svapnavuddhAntayorvAsanApratyayarUpAM nityameva pashyandR^iShTerdraShTA bhavati /

tadbrahma AtmAnameva nityadR^igrUpamadhyAropitAnityadR^iShTyAdivarjitamevAvedviditavat /
nanu vipratiShiddhaM"na vij~nAtevij~nAtAraM vijAnIyAH"(bR^i.u.3 / 4 / 2) iti shruteH, vij~nAturvij~nAnam /
na, evaM vij~nAnAnna vipratiShedhaH /
evaM dR^iShTerdraShTeti vij~nAyata eva /
anyaj~nAnAnapekShatvAcca - na ca draShTurnityaiva dR^iShTirityevaM vij~nAte draShTriviShayAM dR^iShTimanyAmAkAN^kShate /
nivartate hi draShTuviShayadR^iShTyAkAN^kShA tadasambhavAdeva /
na hyavidyamAne viShaya AkAN^kShA kasyacidupajAyate /
na ca dR^ishyA dR^iShTirdraShTAraM viShayIkartumutsahate, yatastAmAkAN^kSheta /
na ca svarUpaviShayAkhAN^kShAsvasyaiva /
tasmAdaj~nAnAdhyAropaNanivR^ittireva'atmAnamevAvet ityuktam,nAtmano viShayIkaraNam' /
tatkathamavet? ityAha - ahaM dR^iShTerdraShTA AtmA brahmAsmi bhavAmIti brahmeti - yatsAkShAdaparokShAtsarvAntara AtmA ashanAyAdyatIto neti netyasthUlamanaNvityevamAdi lakShaNam, tadevAhamasmi, nAnyaH saMsArI, yathA bhavAnAheti /
tasmAdevaM vij~nAnAttadbrahma sarvamabhavat /
tasmAdyuktameva manuShyA manyante yadbrahmavidyayA sarvaM bhaviShyAma iti /
yatpR^iShTam,'kimu tadbrahmAved yasmAttatsarvamabhavat'iti, tannirNItam -'brahma vA idamagra AsIt tadAtmAnamevAvedahaM brahmAsmIti tasmAttatsarvamabhavat'iti /
tattatra yo yo devAnAM madhye pratyabudhyata pratibuddhvAnAtmAnaM yathoktena AtmA tadbrahmAbhavat /
tatharpINAM tathA manuShyANAM ca madhye /
devAnAmityAdi lokadR^iShTyapekShayA na brahmatvabuddhyocyate /
'puraH puruSha Avishat'iti sarvatra brahmaivAnupraviShTamityAdyucyate /
paramArthatastu tatra tatra brahmaivAgra AsItprAkpratibodhAd devAdisharIreshvanyathaiva vibhAvyamAnam /
tadAtmAnamevAvettathaiva ca sarvamabhavat /
asyA brahmavidyAyAH sarvabhAvApattiH phalamityetasyArthasya draDhimne mantrAnudAharati shrutiH /
katham? tad brahma etadAtmAnameva'ahamasmi'iti pashyannetasmAdeva brahmaNo darshanAdR^iShTirvAmadevAkhyaH pratipede ha pratipannavAnkila /
sa etasminmantrAndadarsha -'ahaM manurabhavaM sUryashca'ityAdIn /
tadetadbrahma pashyan iti brahmavidyA parAmR^ishyate /
'ahaM manurabhavaM suryashca'ityAdinA sarvabhAvApattiM brahmavidyAphalaM parAmR^ishati /
pashyansarvAtmabhAvaM phalaM pratipeda ityasmAtprayogAd brahmavidyAsahAyasAdhanasAdhyaM mokShaM darshayati;bhuJNjAnastR^ipyatIti yadvat /
seyaM brahmavidyayA sarvabhAvApattirAsInmahatAM devAdInAM vIryAtishayAt /
nedAnImaidaMyugInAnAM visheShato manuShyANAm, alpavIryatvAditi syAtkasyacidbuddhiH, tadutthApanAyAha- tadidaM prakR^itaM brahma yatsarvabhUtAnupraviShTaM dR^iShTikriyAdiliN^gam, etarhyetasminnapi vartamAnakAle yaH kashcidvyAvR^ittabAhyautsukya AtmAnamevaivaM veda'ahaM brahmAsmi'iti apohyopAdhijanitabhrAntivij~nAnAdhyAropitAnvisheShAn saMsAradharmAnAgandhitamanantaramabAhyaM brahyevAhamasmi kevalamiti-so 'vidyAkR^itAsarvatvanivR^itterbrahAvijhAnAdidaM sarva bhavati /
na hi mahAvIryeShu vAmaDhevAdiShu hInavIryeShu vA vArtamAnikeShu manuShyeShubrahyaNo visheShastadvijhAnasya vAsti /
vArtamAnikeShu puruSheShu tu bahyavidyAphale anaikAntikatA shaDkyata ityata Aha-tasya ha brahyavijhAturyathotkena vidhinA devA mahAvIryAshca nApi abhUtatya.abhavanAya brahyAsarvamAvasya, neshate na paryAptAH, kimutAnye /
brahyAvidyAphalaprApyau vidhnakaraNe devAdaya Ishata iti kA shaDkA? ityucyate-devAdInprati R^iNavattvAnmartyAnAm /
"brahyacaryeNa R^ipibhyo yajhena devabhyaH prajayA pitR^ibhyaH"iti hi jAyamAnamevarNavantaM puruShaM darshayati shrutiH /
pashunidarshanAcca"atho 'yaM vA"(bR^i.u. 1 / 4 / 16) ityAdlokashruteshcAtmano vR^ittiparipipAlayiShayAdhamarNAnivaM devAH paratantrAnmanuShyAnpratyamR^itatvaprAptiM prati vidhnaM kuryuriti nyAyyaivaiShA shaDkA /
svapashUnsvasharIrANIva ca rakShanti devAH /
mahattarAM hi vR^ittiM karmAdhInAM darshayShyati devAdInAM bahupashusamatayaikaikasya puruShasya /
"tasmAndepAM tanna priyaM yadetanmanudhyA vidyAH"(1 / 4 / 10) iti hahi vakShyati /
"yathA ha vai svAya lokAyAriShTimicchedevaM haivaMvide sarvANi bhUtAnyariShTimicchanti"(1 / 4 / 16) iti ca /
brahyAvishve pArArthyanivR^itterna svalokatvaM pashutvaJNcetyamiprAyo 'priyAriShTivacanAbhyAmavagamyate /
tasmAdbrahyAvido brahyavidyAphalarprApta prati kuryureva vidhnaM devAH, prabhAvavantashca hi te /
nanvevaM satyanyAsvapi karmaphalaprAptipudevAnAM vidhnakaraNaMpeyapAnasamam /
hanta tarhyAvisrambho 'bhyudayaniHshreyasasAdhanA. nuShThAneShu /
tatheshvarasyAcintaya. shaktitvAdvidhnakaraNe prabhutvam /
tathA kAlakarmamantrauShadhitapasAm /
eShAM hi phalasampattivipattihetutvaM shAstre loke ca prasidvam /
ato 'pyanAshvAsaH shAstrArthAnuShThAne /
na;sarvapadArthAnAM niyatanimittopAdAnAt, jagadvaicitryadarshanAcca /

karma hi shubhAshubhaM puruShANAM devakAleshvarAdikArakamanapekShya nAtmAnaM prati labhate, labdhAtmakamapi phaladAne 'samartham, kriyAyA hi kArakAdyanekanimittopAdAnasvAbhAvyAt /
tasmAtkriyAnuguNA hi deveshvarAdaya iti karmasu tAvanna phalaprAptiM pratyavisrambhaH /
karmaNAmapyeShAM vashAnigatvaM kvacit, svasAmarthyasyApraNodyatvAt /
karmakAladaivadravyAdisvabhAvAnAM guNapradhAnabhAvastvaniyato durvij~neyashceti tatkR^ito moho lokasya - karmaiva kArakaM nAnyatphalaprAptAviti kecitaM;daivamevetyapare;kAla ityeke;dravyAdisvabhAva iti kecit;sarva ete saMhatA evetyapare /
tatra karmaNaH prAdhAnyamaN^gIkR^itya vedasmR^itivAdAH -"puNyo vai puNyena karmaNA bhavati pApaH pApena"(bR^i.u.3 / 2 / 13) ityAdayaH /
yadyapyeShAM svaviShaye kasyacitprAdhAnyodbhava itareShAM tatkAlInaprAdhAnyashaktistambhaH, tathApi na karmaNaH phalaprAptiM pratyanaikAntikatvam, shAstranyAyanirdhAritatvAtkarmaprAdhAnyasya /
na;avidyApagamamAtratvAd brahmaprAptiphalasya - yaduktaM brahmaprAptiphalaM prati devA vighnaM kuryuriti, tatra na devAnAM vighnakaraNe sAmarthyam;kasmAt? vidyAkAlAnantaritatvAd brahmaprAptiphalasya /
katham? yathA loke draShTushcakShuSha Alokena saMyogo yatkAlaH, tatkAla eva rUpAbhivyaktiH /
evamAtmaviShayaM vij~nAnaM yatkAlam, tatkAla eva tadviShayaj~nAnatirobhAvaH syAt /
ato brahmavidyAyAM satyAmavidyAkAryAnupapatteH pradIpa iva tamaHkAryasya, kena kasya vighnaM kuryurdevAH - yatrAtmatvameva devAnAM brahmavidaH /
tadetadAha - AtmA svarUpaM dhyeyaM yattatsarvashAstrairvij~neyaM brahma, hi yasmAt, eShAM devAnAm, sabrahmavidbhavati /
brahmavidyAsamakAlamevAvidyAmAtravyavadhAnApagamAcchuktikAyA iva rajatAbhAsAyAH shuktikAtvamityavocAma /
ato nAtmanaH pratikUlatve devAnAM prayatnaH sambhavati /
yasya hyanAtmabhUtaM phalaM deshakAlanimittAntaritam, tatrAnAtmaviShaye saphalaH prayatno vighnAcaraNAya devAnAm /
na tviha vidyAsamakAla AtmabhUte deshakAlanimittAnantarite, avasarAnupapatteH /
evaM tarhi vidyApratyayasantatyabhAvAd viparItapratyayatatkAryayoshca darshanAd antya evAtmapratyayo 'vidyAnivartako na tu pUrva iti /
na;prathamenAnaikAntikatvAt /

evaM tarhi santato 'vidyAnivartako na vicchinna iti /
na, jIvanAdau sati santatyanupapatteH /

atha jIvanAdipratyayatiraskaraNenaiva AmaraNAntAdvidyAsantatiriti cenna, pratyayeyattAsamantAnAnavadhAraNAcchAstrArthAnavadhAraNadoShAt /

santatimAtratve 'vadhArita eveti cet? na, AdyantayoravisheShAt /
prathamA vidyApratyayasantatirmaraNakAlAntA veti visheShAbhAvAt, AdyantayoH pratyayoH pUrvoktau doShau prasajyeyAtAm /
evaM tarhyanivartaka eveti cet? na,"tasmAttatsarvamabhavat"(bR^i.u.1 / 4 / 10) iti shruteH /
"bhidyate hR^idayagranthiH"(mu.u.2 / 2 / 8) "tatra ko mohaH" (IshA.7) ityAdi shrutibhyashca /
arthavAda iti cet? na, sarvashAkhopaniShadaH /
pratyakShapramitAtmaviShayatvAdastyeveti cet? na, uktaparihAratvAt /

tasmAdAdyo 'ntyaH santato 'santatashcetyacodyametat /
avidyAdidoShanivR^ittiphalAvasAnatvAdvidhAyAH /
ya evAvidyAdidoShanivR^ittiphalakR^itpratyaya Adyo 'ntyaH santato 'santato vA sa eva vidyetyabhyupagamAnna codyasyAvatAragandho 'pyasti /
yattUktaM viparItapratyayatatkAryayoshca darshanAditi, na;taccheShasthitihetutvAt /
yena karmaNA sharIramArabdhaM tadviparItapratyayadoShanimittatvAttasya tathAbhUtasyaiva viparItapratyayadoShasaMyuktasya phaladAne sAvarthyamiti, yAvaccharIrapAtaH tAvatphalopabhogAN^gatayA viparItapratyayaM rAgAdidoShaM ca tAvanmAtramAkShipatyeva, mukteShuvatpravR^ittaphalatvAttaddhetukasya karmaNaH /
tena na tasya nivartukA vidyA, avirodhAt /

atItaM hItarat /

"kShIyante cAsya karmANi"(mu.u.2 / 2 / 8) "tasya tAvadeva ciram"(chA.u.6 / 14 / 2) "sarve pApmAnaH pradrUyante"(chA.u.5 / 24 / 3) "taM viditvA na lipyate karmaNA pApakena"(bR^i.u.4 / 4 / 23) "etamu haivaite na tarataH"(4 / 4 / 22) "nainaM kR^itAkR^ite tapataH"(4 / 4 / 22) "etaM ha vAva na tapati"(tai.u.2 / 9 / 1) "na bibheti kutashcana"(tai.u.2 / 9 / 1) ityAdi shrutibhyashca /

tadyathehaiva  tAvat - atha yaH kashcidabrahmavid  anyAmAtmAno vyatiriktAM yAM kAJNciddevatAm, upAste stutinamaskArayAgabalyupahArapraNidhAnAdinA upa Aste - anyo 'sAvanAtmA mattaH pR^ithak, anyo 'hamasmyadhikR^itaH, mayAsmai R^iNivatpratikartavyam - ityevampratyayo veda vijAnAti tattvam /
na sa kevalamevaMbhUto 'vidvAnavidyAdoShavAneva, kiM tarhi? yathA pashurgavAdirvAhanadohanAdyupakArairupabhujyate, evaM sa ijyAdyanekopakArairupabhoktavyatvAdekaikena devAdInAm, ataH pashuriva sarvArtheShu karmasvadhikR^ita ityarthaH /
etasya hyaviduSho varNAshramAdipravibhAgavato 'dhikR^itasya karmaNo vidyAsahitasya kevalasya ca shAstroktasya kAryaM manuShyatvAdiko brahmAnta utkarShaH /

sarvAhIyamupaniShad vidyAvidyAvibhAgapradarshanenaivopakShINA /
yathA caiShor'thaH kR^itsnasya shAstrasya tathA pradarshayiShyAmaH /

#<brahma vA idam agra AsId ekam eva |
tad ekaM san na vyabhavat |
tac chreyo rUpam atyasR^ijata kShatraM, yAny etAni devatrA kShatrANIndro varuNaH somo rudraH parjanyo yamo mR^ityur IshAna iti |

BrhUpBh_1,4.11 sUtritaH shAsrArthaH"AtmetyevopAsIta"iti /
tasya ca vyAcikhyAsitasyasArthavAdena"tadAhuryadbrahmavidyayA" ityAdinA sambandhaprayojane abhihite /
avidyAyAshcasaMsArAdhikArakAraNatvamuktam"atha yo 'nyAM devatAmupAste"ityAdinA /
tatrAvidvAnR^iNI pashavaddevAdikarmakartavyatayA paratantra ityuktam /
kiM punardevAdikarmavyatvenimittam? varNA AshramAshca /
tatra ke varNAH? ityataidamArabhyate /
yannimittasambaddheShu karmasvayaM paratantra evAdhikR^itaH saMsArIti /
etasyaivArthasya pradarshanAyAgnisargAnantaramindrAdisargo noktaH /
agnestu sargaH prajApateH sR^iShTiparipUraNAya pradarshitaH /
ayaM ca indrAdisargastatraiva draShTavyastaccheShatvAt /
iha tu sa evAmidhIyate 'viduShaH karmAdhikArahetupradarshanAya- brahma vA idamagra AsIdyadagniM sR^iShTvA agnirUpApannaM brahma /
brAhmaNajAtyamimAnAd brahmetyabhidhIyate /
vai idaM kShatrAdijjAtaM brahmaivAbhinnamAsIdekameva /
nAsItkShatrAdibhedaH /
tadbrahmaikaM kShatrAdiparipAlayitrAdishUnyaM sadaM na vyabhavat- na vibhUtavat, karmaNe nAlamAsIdityarthaH /
tatastadbrahma'brAhmaNo 'smi mametthaM kartavyam'iti brAhmaNajAtinimittaM karma cikIrShu-AtmanaH karmakartR^itvavibhUtyai shreyorUpaM prashastarUpam atyasR^ijatAtishayenAsR^ijata-sR^iShTavat /
kiM punastadyatsR^iShTam? kShatraM kShatriyajAtiH, tadvyaktibhedena pradarshayati-yAnyetAni prasiddhAni loke devatrA deveShu kShatrANIti /
jAtyAkhyAyAM pakShe bahuvacanasmaraNAd vyaktibahutvAdvA bhedopacAreNa bahuvacanam /
kAni punastAni? ityAhatatrAbhipiktA eva visheShato nirdishyante-indro devAnAM rAjA, varuNo yAdasAm, somo brAhmaNAnAm, rudraH pashUnAm, parjanyo vidyudAdInAm, yamaH pitÌNAm, mR^ityurogAdInAm, IshAnobhAsAm-ityevamAdIni deveShukShatrANi /
tadanu, indrAdikShatradevatAdhiShThitAni purUravaHprabhR^itIni sR^iShTAnyeva draShTavyAni /
tadartha eva hi devakShatrasargaH prastutaH /
yasmAdbrahmaNAtishayena sR^iShTaM kShatraM tasmAtkShatrAtparaM nAsti brAhmaNajAterapi niyansR^i /
tasmAdbrAhmaNaH kAraNabhAto 'pi kShatriyasya kShatriyamadhastAdvyavasthitaH sannuparisthitamupAste /
kka? rAjasUye /
kShatra eva tadAtmIyaM yashaH khyAtirUpaM brahmeti dadhAti sthApayati /
rAjasUyAbhiShiktenAsandyAM sthitena rAj~nA Amantrito brahmanniti R^itvikpunastaM pratyAha"tvaM rAjanbrahmAsi"iti /
tadetadabhidhIyate -"kShatra eva tadyasho dadhAti"iti /
saiShA prakR^itA kShatrasya yonireva yadbrahma /
tasmAdyadyati rAjA paramatAM rAjasUyAbhiShekaguNaM gacchatyApnoti brahmaiva brAhmaNajAtimedha, antato 'nte karmaparisamAptAvupanikShayatyAshrayati svAM yonim, purohitaM puro nidhatta ityarthaH /
yastu punarbalAbhimAnAtsvAM yoniM brAhmaNajAtiM brAhmaNaM ya u enaM hinasti hiMsati nyagbhAvena pashyati, svAmAtmAyAmeva sa yonimR^icchati-svaM prasavaM vicchinatti vinAshayati-svaM prasavaM vicchinatti vinAshayati /
sa etatkR^itvA pApIyAnpApataro bhavati /
pUrvamapi kShatriyaH pApa eva krUratvAdAtmaprasavahiMsayA sutarAm /
yathA loke shreyAMsaM prashastataraM hiMsitvA paribhUya pApataro bhavati tadvat //11//



kShatre sR^iShTe 'pi-

#<tad etad brahma kShatraM viT shUdraH |

BrhUpBh_1,4.15 tadetaccAturvarNyaM sR^iShTam - brahma kShatraM viTshUdra iti;uttarArthaM upasaMhAraH yattatsraShTR^i brahma, tadagninaivanAnyena rUpeNa deveShu brahma, brAhmaNajAtirabhavat /

yatra nu devAdhInA puruShArthasiddhiH, tatraivAgnyAdisambaddhakriyApekShA /
