kuryAdanyanna vA kuryAnmaitro brAhmaNa ucyate //
" (manu.2 / 87) iti /
pArivrAjyadarshanAcca /
tasmAdbrahmaNatva eva manuShyeShu lokaM karmaphalamicchanti /
yasmAdetAbhyAM hi brAhmaNAgnirUpAbhyAM karmakartradhikaraNarUpAbhyAM yatsraShTR^i brahma sAkShAdabhavat /
atra tu paramAtmalokamagnau brAhmaNe cecchantIti kecit /
tadasat, avidyAdhikAre karmAdhikArArthaM varNavibhAgasya prastutatvAt, pareNa ca visheShaNAt;yadi hyatra lokashabdena para evAtmocyeta, pareNa visheShaNamanarthakaM syAt'svaM lokamadR^iShTvA'iti /
svalokavyatiriktashcedagnyadhInatayA prArthyamAnaH prakR^ito lokaH, tataH svam, iti yuktaM visheShaNam, prakR^itaparalokanivR^ittyarthatvAt;svatvena cAvyabhicArAtparamAtmalokasya, avidyAkR^itAnAM ca svatvavyabhicArAt /
bravIti ca karmakR^itAnAM vyabhicAram-'kShIyata eva'iti /
brahmaNA sR^iShTA varNAH karmArtham;tacca karma dharmAkhyaM sarvAneva kartavyatayA niyantR^i puruShArthasAdhanaM va /
tasmAttenaiva cetkarmaNA svo lokaH paramAtmAkhyo 'vidito 'pi prApyate, kiM tasyaiva padanIyatvena kriyata ityata Aha-atheti pUrvapakShavinivR^ittyarthaH;yaH kashcit, ha vai asmAtsaMsArikAmakarmahetukAdagnyadhInakarmAbhimAnatayA vA brAhmaNajAtimAtrakarmAbhimAnatayA vA AgantukAdasvabhUtAllokAt, svaM lokamAtmAkhyam AtmatvenAvyabhicAritvAt, adR^iShTA -'ahaM brahmAsmi'iti, praiti mriyate;sa yadyapi svo lokaH, avidito 'vidyayA vyavahito 'sva ivAj~nAtaH enam - saN^khyApUraNa iva laukika AtmAnam na bhunakti na pAlayati shokamohabhayAdidoShApanayena /
yathA ca loke vedo 'nanukto 'nadhItaH karmAdyavabodhakatvena na bhunakti, anyadvA laukikaM kR^iShyAdi karmAkR^itaM svAtmanAnabhivyaJNjitam AtmIyaphalapradAnena na bhunakti, evamAtmA svo lokaH svenaiva nityAtmasvarUpeNAnabhivyaJNjito 'vidyAdi prahANena na bhunaktyeva /
nanu kiM svalokadarshananimittaparipAlanena? karmaNaH phalaprAptidhrauvyAt, iShTaphalanimittasya ca karmaNo bAhulyAt, tannimittaM pAlanamakShayaM bhaviShyati /
tanna, kR^itasya kShayavattvAt;ityetadAha - yadiha vai saMsAre 'dbhutavatkashcinmahAtmApi, anevaMvit-svaM lokaM yathoktena vidhinA avidvAn, mahadbahu ashvamedhAdi puNyaM karma iShTaphalameva nairantaryeNa karoti,'anenaivAnantyaM mama bhaviShyati'iti, tatkarma hAsyAvidyAvato 'vidyAjanitakAmahetutvAt svapnadarshanavibhramodbhUtavibhUtivadantato 'nte phalopabhogasya kShIyata eva /
tatkAraNayoravidyAkAmayoshcalatvAt, kR^itakShayaghnauvyopapattiH /
tasmAnna puNyakarmaphalapAlanAnantyAshA astyeva /
ata AtmAnameva svaM lokam -'AtmAnam'iti'svaM lokam'ityasminnarthe, svaM lokamiti prakR^itatvAt, iha ca svashabdasyAprayogAt - upAsIta /
sa ya AtmAnameva lokamupAste, tasya kim? ityucyate - na hAsya karma kShIyate;karmAbhAvAdeva, iti nityAnuvAdaH /
yathAviduShaH karmakShayalakShaNaM saMsAraduHkhaM santatameva,na tathA tadasya vidyata ityarthaH /
"mithilAyAM pradIptAyAM na me dahyati kiJNcana"iti yadvat /
svAtmalokopAsakasya viduSho vidyAsaMyogAtkarmaiva na kShIyata ityapare varShayanti /
lokashabdArthaM ca karmasamavAyinaM dvidhA parikalpayanti kila eko vyAkR^itAvasthA karmAshrayo loko hairaNyagarbhAkhyaH, taM karmasamavAyinaM lokaM vyAkR^itaM paricchinnaM ya upAste, tasya kila paricchinnaM ya upAste, tasya kila paricchinnakarmAtmadarshinaH karma kShIyate /
tameva karmasamavAyinaM lokamavyAkR^itAvasthaM kAraNarUpamApAdya yastUpAste, tasyAparicchinnakarmAtmadarshitvAttasya yastUpAste, tasyAparicchinnakarmAtmadarshitvAttasya karma na kShIyata iti /
bhavatIyaM shobhanA kalpanA na tu shrautI /
svalokashabdena prakR^itasya paramAtmano 'bhihitatvAt /
svaM lokamiti prastutya svashabdaM vihAyAtmashabdaprakShepeNa punastasyaiva pratinirdeshAdAtmAnameva lokamupAsIteti /
tatra karmasamavAyilokakalpanAyA anavasara eva /
pareNa ca kevalavidyAviShayeNa visheShaNAt -"kiM prajayA kariShyAmo yeShAM no 'yamAtmAyaM lokaH"(bR^i.u.4 / 4 / 22) ithi /
putrakarmAparavidyAkR^itebhyo hi lokebhyo vishinaShTi'ayamAtmA no lokaH'iti /
"na hAsya kenacana karmaNA loko mIyata eSho 'sya paramo lokaH"iti ca /

sarvAtmabhAvapradarshanArtho vA pUrvavat /
yadi hi para evAtmA sampadyate tadA yuktaH asmAddhyevAtmanaH ityAtmashabdaprayogaH, svasmAdeva prakR^itAdAtmano lokAdityevamarthaH /
anyathA'avyAkR^itAvasthAtkarmaNo lokAt'iti savisheShaNamavakShyAt prakR^itaparamAtmalokavyAvR^ittaye vyAkR^itAvasthAvyAvR^ittaye ca /
na hyasminprakR^ite visheShite 'shrutAntarAlAvasthApratipattuM shakyate //15//

BrhUpBh_1,4.17 Atmaivedamagra AsIt /
Atmaiva svAbhAviko 'vidvAnkAryakaraNasaN^ghAtalakShaNo varNI, agre prAgdArasambandhAt,AtmetyabhidhIyate;tasmAdAtmanaH pR^ithagbhUtaM kAmyamAnaM jAyAdibhedarUpaM nAsIt;sa evaika AsIt - jAyAdyeShaNAbIjabhUtA vidyAvAneka evAsIt /
svAbhAvikyA svAtmani kartrAdikArakakriyAphalAtmakatAdhyAropalakShaNayA avidyAvAsanayA vAsitaH so 'kAmayata kAmitavAn /
katham? jAyA karmAdhikArahetubhUtA me mama kartuH syAt;tayA vinAhamanadhikR^ita eva karmaNi;ataH karmAdhikArasampattaye bhavejjAyA;athAhaM prajAyeya prajArUpeNAhamevotpadyeya /
atha vittaM me syAtkarmasAdhanaM gavAdilakShaNam athAhamabhyudayaniHshreyasasAdhanaM karma kurvIya;yenAhamanR^iNI bhUtvA devAdInAM lokAn prApnuyAm, tatkarma kurvIya;kAmyAni ca putravittasvargAdisAdhanAni /
etAvAnvai kAma etAvadviShayaparicchinna ityarthaH /
etAvAneva hi kAmayitavyo viShayo yaduta jAyAputravittakarmANi sAdhanalakShaNaiShaNA;lokAshca trayo manuShyalokaH pitR^iloko devaloka iti phalabhUtAH sAdhanaiShaNA, tasmAtsA ekaivaiShaNA yA lokaiShaNA /
saikaiva satyeShaNA sAdhanApekSheti dvidhA;ato 'vadhArayiShyati"ubhe hyete eShaNe eva"3 / 5 / 1) iti /
phalArthatvAtsarvArambhasya lokaiShaNArthaprAptA uktaiveti /
etAvAnvA etAvAneva kAma ityavadhriyate /
bhojane 'bhihite tR^iptirna hi pR^ithagabhidheyA, tadarthatvAdbhojanasya /
te ete eShaNe sAdhyasAdhanalakShaNe kAmaH, yena prayukto 'vidvAnavasha eva koshakAravadAtmAnaM veShTayati - karmamArga evAtmAnaM praNidadhadbahirmukhIbhUto na svaM lokaM pratijAnAti /
tathA ca taittirIyake -"agnimugdho haiva dhUmatAntaH svaM lokaM na pratijAnAti"iti /
kathaM punaretAvattvamavadhAryate kAmAnAm? anantatvAt /
anantA hi kAmAH, ityetadAshaN^kya hetumAha - yasmAd na icchan ca na icchannapi, ato 'smAtphalasAdhanalakShaNAd bhUyo 'dhikAraM na vindenna labheta /
na hi loke phalasAdhanavyatiriktaM dR^iShTamadR^iShTaM vA labdhavyamasti /
labdhavyaviShayo hi kAmaH, tasya caitadvyatirekeNAbhAvAt yuktaM vaktum'etAvAnvai kAmaH'iti /
etaduktaM bhavati - dR^iShTArthamadR^iShTArtha vA sAdhyasAdhanalakShaNam avidyAvatpuruShAdhikAraviShayameShaNAdvayaM kAmaH, ato 'smAdviduShA vyutthAtavyamiti /
yasmAdevamavidvAnAtmA kAmo pUrvaM kAmayAmAsa, tathA pUrvataro 'pi, eShA lokasthitiH prajApateshcaivameSha sargaM AsIt /
so 'bibhedavidyayA, tataH kAmaprayukta ekAkyaramamANo 'styupaghAtAya striyamaicchat, tAM samabhavat tataH sargo 'yamAsIditi hyuktam /
tasmAttatsR^iShTau etarhyetasminnapi kAla ekAkI sanprAgdArakriyAtaH kAmayate - jAyA me syAt, atha prajAyeya atha vittaM me syAt, atha karma kurvIya - ityuktArthaM vAkyam /
sa evaM kAmayamAnaH sampAdayaMshca jAyAdInyAvatsa eteShAM yathoktAnAM jAyAdInAmekaikamapi na prApnoti, akR^itsno 'sampUrNo 'hamityevaM tAvadAtmAnaM manyate /
pArisheShyAtsamastAnevaitAnsampAdayati yadA, tadA tasya kR^itsnatA /
yadA tu na shaknoti kR^itsnatAM sampAdayituM tadA asya kR^itsnatvasampAdanAyAha - tasyo tasyAkR^itsnatvabhimAninaH kR^itsnatA iyam evaM bhavati katham? ayaM kAryakaraNasaN^ghAtaH pravibhajyate;tatra mano 'nuvR^itti hi itaratsarvaM kAryakaraNaj~nAtamiti manaH pradhAnatvAjAtmevAtmA /
yathA jAyAdInAM kuTumbapatirAtmeva tadanukAritvAJNjAyAdi catuShTyasya;evamihApi mana AtmA parikalpate kR^itsnatAyai /
tathA vAgjAyA, mano 'nuvR^ittitvasAmAnyAdvAcaH /
vAgiti shabdashcodanAdilakShaNaH, manasA shrotradvAreNa gR^ihyate 'vadhAryate prasR^ijyate ca, iti manaso jAyeva vAk /
tAbhyAM ca vAÇmanasAbhyAM jAyApatisthAnIyAbhyAM prasUyate prANaH karmArtham, iti prANaH prajeva /
tatra prANaceShTAdilakShaNaM karma cakShurmAnuShaM vittam /
tad dvividhaM vittaM mAnuShamitaracca;ato vishinaShTItaravittanivR^ittyartha mAnuShamiti /
gavAdi hi manuShyasambandhi vittaM cakShurgrAhyaM karmasAdhanam;tasmAttatsthAnIyam, tena sambandhAccakShurgrAhyaM vittam;cakShuShA hi yasmAttanmAnuShaM vittaM vindate gavAdyupalabhata ityarthaH /
kiM punaritaradvittam? shrotraM daivaM devaviShayatvAdvij~nAnasya /
vij~nAnaM daivaM vittam;tadiha shrotrameva sampattiviShayam /
kasmAt? shrotreNa hi yasmAttaddaivaM vittaM vij~nAnaM shR^iNoti;ataH shrotrameva taditi /
kiM punaretairAtmAdivittAntairiha nirvartya karma? ityucyate - Atmaiva - Atmeti sharIramucyate /
kathaM punarAtmA karmasthAnIyaH? asya karmahetutvAt /
kathaM karmahetutvam? AtmanA hi sharIreNa yataH karma karoti /
tasyAkR^itsnatvAbhimAnina evaM kR^itsnatA sampannA - yathA bAhyA jAyAdilakShaNA evam /
tasmAtsa eSha pAN^ktaH paJNcabhirnirvR^ittaH pAN^kto yaj~no darshanamAtranirvR^itto 'karmiNo 'pi /
kathaM punarasya paJNcatvasampattimAtreNa yaj~natvam? ucyate - yasmAdbAhyo 'pi yaj~naH pashupuruShasAdhyaH, sa ca pashuH puruShashca pAN^kta eva yathoktamanaAdipaJNcatvayogAt /
tadAha - pAN^ktaH pashugarvAdiH, pAN^ktaH puruShaH pashutve 'pyadhikR^itatvenAsya visheShaH puruShasyeti pR^ithakpuruShagrahaNam /
kiM bahunA? pAN^ktamidaM sarvaM karmasAdhanaM phalaM ca, yadidaM kiJNca yatkiJNcididaM sarvam /
evaM pAN^ktaM yaj~namAtmAnaM yaH sampAdayat sa tadidaM sarvaM jagadAtmatvenApnoti ya evaM veda //17//

#<iti prathamAdhyAye caturthaM sR^iShTyAdisarvAtmatAbrAhmaNam //4//>#



yatsaptAnnAni medhayA /
avidyA prastutA, tatrAvidvAnanyAM devatAmupAste'anyo 'sAvanyo 'hamasmi'iti /
sa varNAshramAbhimAnaH karmakartavyatayA niyato juhotyAdikarmabhiH kAmaprayukto devAdInAmupakurvansarveShAM bhUtAnAM loka ityuktam /
yathA ca svakarmabhirekaikena sarvairbhUtairasau loko bhojyatvena sR^iShTaH, evamasAvapi juhotyAdipAN^ktakarmabhiH sarvANi bhUtAni sarvaM ca jagadAtmabhojyatvenAsR^ijat /
evamekaikaH svakarmavidyAnurUpyeNa sarvasya jagato bhoktA bhojyaM ca, sarvasya sarvaH kartA kAryaM cetyarthaH /
etadeva ca vidyAprakaraNe madhuvidyAyAM vakShyAmaH -'sarvaM sarvasya kAryaM madhu'ityAtmaikatvavij~nAnArtham /
yadasau juhotItyAdinA pAN^ktena kAmyena karmaNA Atmabhojyatvena jagadasR^ijata vij~nAnena ca, tajjagatsarvaM saptadhA pravibhajyamAnaM kAryakAraNatvena saptAnnAnyucyante, bhojyatvAt;tenAsau pitA teShAmannAnAm /
eteShAmannAnAM saviniyogAnAM sUtrabhUtAH saN^kShepataH prakAshakatvAdime mantrAH /

START BrhUp 1,5.1

#<yat saptAnnAni medhayA tapasAjanayat pitA |

BrhUpBh_1,5.1 yatsaptAnnAni, yad ajanayaditi kriyAvisheShaNam;medhayA praj~nayA vij~nAnena tapasA ca karmaNA;j~nAnakarmaNI eva hi medhAtapaH shabdavAcye, tayoH prakR^itatvAt;netare medhAtapasI, aprakaraNAt;pAN^ktaM hi karma jAyAdisAdhanam; 'ya evaM veda'iti cAnantarameva j~nAnaM prakR^itam;tasmAnna prasiddhayormedhAtapasorAshaN^kA kAryA;ato yAni saptAnnAni j~nAnakarmabhyAM janitavAnpitA tAni prakAshayiShyAma iti vAkyasheShaH //1//

START BrhUp 1,5.2

#<yat saptAnnAni medhayA tapasAjanayat piteti |

BrhUpBh_1,5.2 tatra'yatsaptAnnAni medhayA tapasAjanayatpitA'ityasya kor'tha ucyate? ithi hi shabdenaiva vyAcaShTe prasiddhArthAvadyotakena /
prasiddho hyasya mantrasyArtha ityarthaH /
yadajanayaditi cAnuvAdasvarUpeNa mantreNa prasiddhArthataiva prakAshitA /
ato brAhmaNamavishaN^kyaivAha -'medhayA hi tapasAjanayatpitA'iti? nanu kathaM prasiddhAtAsyArthasya? ityucyate - jAyAdikarmAntAnAM lokaphalasAdhanAnAM pitR^itvaM tAvat pratyakShameva, abhihitaM ca'jAyA me syAt'ityAdinA /
tatra ca daivaM vittaM vidyA karma putrashca phalabhUtAnAM lokAnAM sAdhanaM sraShTR^itvaM pratItyabhihitam, vakShyamANaM ca prasiddhameva;tasmAdyuktaM vaktuM medhayetyAdi /
eShaNA hi phalaviShayA prasiddhaiva ca loke /
eShaNA ca jAyAdItyuktam'etAvAnvai kAmaH'ityanena /
brahmavidyAviShaye ca sarvaikatvAtkAmAnupapatteH /
etenAshAstrIyapraj~nAtapobhyAM svAbhAvikAbhyAM jagatsraShTR^itvamuktameva bhavati;sthAvarAntasya cAniShTaphalasya karmavij~nAnanimittatvAt /
vivakShitastu shAstrIya eva sAdhyasAdhanabhAvo brahmavidyAvidhitsayA tadvairAgyasya vivakShitatvAt /
sarvo hyaM vyaktAvyaktalakShaNaH saMsAro 'suddho 'nityaH sAdhyasAdhanarUpo duHkho 'vidyAviShaya ityetasmAdviraktasya brahmavidyA Arabdhavyeti /
tatrAnnAnAM vibhAgena viniyoga ucyate-'ekamasya sAdhAraNma'iti mantrapadam, tasya vyAkhyAnam'idamevAsya tasmAdhAraNamannam'ityuttkam /
asya bhottkR^isamudAyasya, kiM tat? yadidamadyate bhujyate sarvaiH prANibhirahanyahani, tasmAdhAraNaM sarvabhoktrarthamakalpayatpitA sR^iShTvAnnam /
sa ya etatsAdhAraNaM sarvaprANabhR^itsthitikaraM bhujyamAnamannamupAste tatparo bhavatItyarthaH-- upAsanaM hi nAma tAtparya dR^iShTaM loke'gurumupAste' 'rAjAnamupAste'ityAdau--tasmAccharIrasthityarthannopabhogapradhAnonAdR^iShTArthakarmapradhAna ityarthaH;sa evaM bhUto na pApmano 'dharmadvayAvartate--na vimucyata ityetat /
tathA ca mantravarNaH---"moghamannaMvindate"ityAdiH /
smR^itirapi-"nAtmArtha pAcayedannam" "apradAyaibhyo yo bhUN^kte stena eva saH" "annAde bhrUNahA mArShTi" ityAdiH /
kasmAtpunaH pApmano na vyAvartate? mishraM hyetasmarseShAM hi svaM tadapravibhaktaM yatprANibhirbhujyate /
sarvabhojyatpAdeva yo mukhe prakShipyamANo 'pi grAsaH parasya pIDAkaro dR^ishyate,'mamedaM syAt'iti hi sarveShAM tatrAshA prativadvA /
tasmAnna paramapIDaytvA grasitumapi shakyate /
"duShkR^itaM hi manuShyANAm"ityAdismaraNAcca /
gR^ihiNA vaishvadevAkhyamannaM yadahanyahani nirUpyata iti kecit, tatra, sarvabhottakR^isAdhAraNatvaM vaishvadevAkhyasyAnnasya na sarvaprANabhR^idbhujyamAnAnnavatpratyakSham, nApi'yadidamadyate'iti tadviShayaM vacanamanukUlam /
sarvaprANabhR^idbhapajyamAnAMnAnnAntaHpAtitvAcca vaishvadevAkhyasya yuttakaM shvacANDAlAdyAdhasyAnnasya grahaNam, vaishvadevavyatirekeNApi shvacANDAlAdyAdhAshvadarshanAt, tatra yutkam,'yadidamadyate'iti vacanam /
yadi hi tanna gR^ihyeta, sAdhAraNashabdena pitrAsR^iShTatvAviniyuttkatve tasya prasajyeyAtAm /
iShyate hi tatsR^iShTavaM tadviniyuttkatvaM ya sarvasyAnnajAtasya /
na ca vaishvadevAkhyaM shAstroktaM karma kurvataH pApmano 'vinivR^ittiryuktA, na ca tasya pratiShedho 'sti, na ca matsyabandhanAdikarmavatsvabhAvajugupsitametat, shiShTanirvartyatvAt, akaraNe ca pratyavAyashravaNAt /
itaratra ca pratyavAyopapatteH"ahamannamannamadantamA3Çmi"(tai.u.3 / 10 / 6) iti mantravarNAt /
dve devAnabhAjayat iti mantrapadam, ye dve anne sR^iShTvA devAnabhAjayat /
ke te dve? ityucyate - hutaM ca prahutaM ca /
hutamityagnau havanam, prahutaM hutvA baliharaNam /
yasmAd dve ete anne hutaprahute devAnabhAjayatpitA /
tasmAdetarhyapi gR^ihiNaH kAle dvebhyo(? ) juhvati devebhya idamannamasmAbhirdIyamAnamiti manvAnA juhvati, prajuhvati ca hutvA baliharaNaM ca kurvata ityarthaH /
atho apyanya Ahurdve anne pitrA devebhyaH pratte na hutaprahute, kiM tarhi? darshapUrNamAsAviti /
dvitvashravaNAvisheShAdatyantaprasiddhatvAcca hutaprahute iti prathamaH pakShaH /
yadyapi dvitvaM hutaprahutayoH sambhavati, tathApi shrautayoreva tu darshapUrNamAsayordevAnnatvaM prasiddhataram, mantra prakAshitatvAt /
guNapradhAnaprAptau ca pradhAne prathamatarA avagatiH, darshapUrNamAsayoshca prAdhAnyaM hutaprahutApekShayA /
tasmAttayoreva grahaNaM yuktam'dve devAnabhAjayat'iti /
yasmAddevAtamete pitrA prakÊpte darshapUrNamAsAkhye anne, tasmAttayordevArthatvAvighAtAya neShTiyAjuka iShTiyajanashIlaH, iShTishabdena kila kAmyA iShTayaH, shAtapathIyaM prasiddhiH, tAcchIlyapratyayaprayogAtkAmyeShTiyajanapradhAne na syAdityarthaH /
pashubhya ekaM prAyacchaditi - yatpashubhya  ekaM punastadannam? tatpayaH /
kathaM punaravagamyate pashavo 'syAnnasya svAminaH? ityata Aha - payo hyagre prathamaM yasmAnmanuShyAshca pashavashca payaH evopajIvantIti /
ucitaM hi'tapo tadannam'anyathA kathaM tadevAgre niyamenopajIveyuH? kathamagre tadevopajIvanti? ityucyate - manuShyAshca pashavashca yasmAttenaivAnnena vartante 'dyatve 'pi, yathA pitrA Adau viniyogaH kR^itastathA /
tasmAtkumAraM bAlaM jAtaM ghR^itaM vA traivarNikA jAtakarmaNi jAtarUpasaMyuktaM pratilehayanti pashcAt pAyayanti /
yathAsambhavamanyeShAM stanamevAgre dhApayanti manuShyebhyo 'nyeShAM pashUnAm /
atha vatsaM jAtamAhuH'kiyatpramANo vatsaH'? ityevaM pR^iShTA- santo 'tR^iNAda iti /
nAdyApi tR^iNamatti, atIva bAlaH, payasaivAdyApi vartata ityarthaH /
yaccAgre jAtakarmAdau ghR^itamupajIvanti, yaccetare paya eva, tatsarvathApi paya evopajIvanti;ghR^itasyApi payovikAratvAtpayastvameva kasmAtpunaH saptamaM satpashvannaM caturthatvena vyAkhyAyate? karmasAdhanatvAt /
karma hi payaHsAdhanAshrayaM agnihotrAdi /
tacca karma sAdhanaM vittasAdhyaM vakShyamANasyAnnatrayasya sAdhyasya, yathA darshapUrNamAsau pUrvoktAvanne /
ataH karmapakShatvAt karmaNA saha piNDIkR^ityopadeshaH /
sAdhanatvAvisheShAdarthasambandhAdAnantaryamakAraNamiti cAvyAkhyAne pratipattisaukaryAcca /
sukhaM hi nairantaryeNa vyAkhyAtu shakyante 'nnAni vyAkhyAtAni ca sukhaM pratIyante /
tasminsarvaM pratiShThitaM yacca prANiti yacca netyasya kor'thaH? ityucyate - tasminpashvanne payasi sarvamadhyAtmAdhibhUtAdhidaivalakShaNaM kR^itsnaM jagatpratiShThitaM yacca prANiti prANaveShTAvadyacca na sthAnaraM shailAdi /
tatra hi shabdenaiva prasiddhAvadyotakena vyAkhyAtam /
kAraNatvApapatteH /
kAraNatvaM cAgnihotrAdikarmasamavAyitvam /
agnihotrAdyAhutivipariNAmAtmakaM ca jagatkR^itsnamiti shrutismR^itivAdAH shatasho vyavasthitAH /
ato yuktameva hi shabdena vyAkhyAnam /
yattadbrAhmaNAntareShvidamAhuH - saMvatsaraM payasA juhvadapa punarmR^ityuM jayatIti, saMvatsareNa kila trINi ShaShTishatAnyAhutInAM sapta ca shatAni viMshatishceti yAjuShmatIriShTakA abhisampadyamAnAH saMvatsarasya cAhorAtrANi, saMvatsaramagniM prajApatimApnuvanti;evaM kR^itvA saMvatsaraM juhvadapajayati punaH mR^ityum, itaH pretya deveShu sambhUtaH punarna mriyata ityarthaH /
ityevaM brAhmaNavAdA AhuH, na tathA vidyAnna tathA draShTavyam;yadahareva juhoti tadahaH punarmR^ityumapajayati, na saMvatsarAbhyAsamapekShate /
evaM vidvAnsan, yaduktam - payasi hIdaM sarvaM pratiShThitaM paya AhutivipariNAmAtmakatvAtsarvasyeti, tadekenaivAhvA jagadAtmatvaM pratipadyate;taducyate - apajayati punarmR^ityuM punarmaraNam, sakR^inmR^itvAviddhAJNcharIreNa viyujya sarvAtmA bhavati na punarmaraNAya paricchinnaM sharIraM gR^ihNAtItyarthaH /
kaH punarhetuH sarvAtmAptyA mR^ityumapajayati? ityucyate - sarvaM samastaM hi yasmAddevebhyaH sarvebhyo 'nnAdyamannameva tadAdyaM ca sAyaMprAtarAhutiprakShepeNa prayacchati /
tadyuktaM sarvamAhutimayamAtmAnaM kR^itvA sarvadevAnnarUpeNa sarvairdevairekAtmabhAvaM gatvA sarvadevamayo bhUtvA punarna mriyata iti /
athaitadapyuktaM brAhmaNena -"brahma vai svayambhU tapo 'tapyata tadaikShata na vai tapasyAnantyamasti, hantAhaM bhUteShvAtmAnaM juhavAni bhUtAni cAtmanIti, tatsarveShu bhUteShvAtmAnaM hutvA bhUtAni cAtmani sarveShAM bhUtAnAM shraiShThyaM svArAjyagAdhipatyaM paryet"iti /
kasmAttAni na kShIyante 'dyamAnAni sarvadeti /
yadA pitrA annAni sR^iShTvA sapta pR^ithakpR^ithagbhoktR^ibhiradyagAnAni - tannimittatvAtteShAM sthiteH - sarvadA nairantaryeNa;kR^itakShayopapatteshca yuktasteShAM kShayaH /
na ca tAni kShIyamANAni, jagato 'vibhraShTarUpeNaivAvasthAnadarshanAt /
bhavitavyaM cAkShayakAraNena;tasmAtkasmAtpunastAni na kShIyanta iti prashnaH /
tasyedaM prativacanam  -'puriSho vA akShitiH' /
yathAsau pUrvamannAnAM sraShTAsItpitA medhayA jAyAdisambandhena ca pAN^ktakarmaNA bhoktA ca, tathA yebhyo dattAnyannAni te 'pi teShAmannAnAM bhoktAro 'pi santaH pitara eva, medhayA tapasA ca yato janayanti tAnyannAni /
tadetadabhidhIyate puruSho vai yo 'nnAnAM bhoktA so 'kShitirakShayahetuH /
kathamasyAkShititvam? ityucyate - sa hi yasmAdidaM bhujyamAnaM saptavidhaM kAryakaraNalakShaNaM kriyAphalAtmakaM punaH punarbhUyo bhUyo janayata utpAdayati dhiyA dhiyA tattatkAlabhAvinyA tayA tayA praj~nayA, karmabhishca vAÇmanaHkAyaveShTitaiH yadyadi ha yadyetatsaptavidhamannamuktaM kShaNamAtramapi na kuryAtpraj~nayA karmabhishca, tato vicchidyeta bhujyamAnatvAtsAtatyena kShIyeta ha /
tasmAdyathaivAyaM puruSho bhoktA annAnAM nairantaryeNa, yathApraj~ne yathAkarma ca karotyapi /
tasmAtpuruSho 'kShitiH sAtatyena kartR^itvAt /
tasmAd bhujyamAnAnyapyannAni na kShIyanta ityarthaH /
ataH praj~nAkriyAlakShaNaprabandhArUDhaH sarvo lokaH sAdhyasAdhanalakShaNaH kriyAphalAtmakaH saMhatAnekaprANikarmavAsanAsantAnAvaShTabdhatvAtkShaNiko 'shuddho 'sAro nadIsrotaH pradIpasantAnakalpaH kadalIstambhavadasAraH phenamAyAmarIcyambhaHsvapnAdisamastadAtmagatadR^iShTInAmavikIryamANo nityaH sAravAniva lakShyate /
tadetadvairAgyArthamucyate - dhiyA dhiyA janayate karmabhiryaddhaitanna kuryAtkShIyeta heti - viraktAnAM hyasmAdbrahmavidyA ArabdhavyA caturthapramukheNeti /
yo vaitAmakShitiM vedeti;vakShyamANAnyapi trINyannAnyasminnavasare vyakhyAtAnyeveti kR^itvA teShAM yAthAtmyavij~nAnaphalamupasaMhriyate - yo vA etAm akShitim akShayahetuM yathoktaM veda, puruSho vA akShitiH sa hIdamannaM dhiyA dhiyA janayate karmabhiryaddhaitanna kuryAtkShIyate heti /
so 'nnamatti pratIkenetyasyArtha ucyate - mukhaM mukhyatvaM prAdhAnyamityetat /
prAdhAnyevAnnAnAM pituH puruShasyAkShititvaM yo veda so 'nnamatti nAnnaM prati guNabhUtaH san /
yathAj~no na tathA vidvAnannAnAyAtmabhUtaH, bhoktaiva bhavati, na bhojyatAmApAdyate /
sa devAnapi gacchati sa UrjamupajIvati, devAnapi gacchati devAtmabhAvaM pratipadyate, UrjamamR^itaM copajIvatIti yaduktaM sA prashaMsA, nApUrvArtho 'nyo 'sti //2//

pAN^ktasya karmaNaH phalabhUtAni yAni trINyannApyupakShiptAni tAni kAryatvAdvistIrNaviShayatvAcca pUrvabhyo 'nnebhyaH pR^ithagutkR^iShTAni, teShAM vyAkhyAnArtha uttaro grantha A brAhmaNaparisamApteH /




_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 1,5.3

#<trINy Atmane 'kuruteti:
mano vAcaM prANaM tAny Atmane 'kuruta |
anyatramanA abhUvaM nAdarsham anyatramanA abhUvaM nAshrauSham iti manasA hy eva pashyati manasA shR^iNoti |
kAmaH saMkalpo vicikitsA shraddhAshraddhA dhR^itir adhR^itir hrIr dhIr bhIr ity etat sarvaM mana eva |
tasmAd api pR^iShThata upaspR^iShTo manasA vijAnAti |
yaH kashca shabdo vAg eva sA |
eShA hy antaM AyattaiShA hi na |
prANo 'pAno vyAna udAnaH samAno 'na ity etat sarvaM prANa eva |
etanmayo vA ayam AtmA |
vAÇmayo manomayaH prANamayaH || BrhUp_1,5.3 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_1,5.3 trINyAtmane 'kuruteti ko 'syArtha ityucyate - manovAkprANA etAni trINyannAni, tAni mano vAcaM prANaM cAtmane AtmArthamakuruta - kR^itavAn sR^iShTvA Adau pitA /
teShAM saMshaya ityata Aha - asti tAvanmanaH shrotrAdibAhyakaraNavyatiriktam, yata evaM prasiddham - bAhyakaraNaviShayAtmasambandhe satyapyabhimukhIbhUtaM viShayaM na gR^ihNAti,'kiM dR^iShTavAnasIdaM rUpam'? ityukto vadati -'anyatra me gataM mana AsItso 'hamanyatramanA AsaM nAdarsham' /
tathA'idaM shrutavAnasi madIyaM vacaH'ityuktaH'anyatramanA abhUvaM nAshrauShaM na shrutavAnasmi'iti /
tasmAd yasyAsannidhau rUpAdigrahaNasamarthasyApi satashcakShurAdeH svasvaviShayasambandhe rUpAshabdAdij~nAnaM na bhavati, yasya ca bhAve bhavati, tadanyadasti mano nAmAntaHkaraNaM sarvakAraNaviShayayogi ityavagabhyate /
tasmAtsarvo hi lokAM manasA hyeva pashyati manasA shR^iNoti, tadvayagratve darshanAdyabhAvAt /
astitve sidve manasaH svarUpArthamidamucyatekAmaH strIcyatikarAbhIlAShAdiH, saMkalpaH pratyupasthitavipayavikalpanaM shuklanIlAdibhedena, vicikitsA saMshayaj~nAnam, shradvA adR^iShTArtheShu karmasvAstikyavudvidaivayAdipu ca, ashradvA tadviparItA vudviH, dhR^itirdhAraNaM dehAdyavasAde uttambhan, adhR^itistadviparyayaH, hrIrlajjA, dhIH praj~nA, bhIrbhayma, ityetadevamAdikaM sarvaM mana eva;manaso 'ntaHkaraNasya rUpANyetAni /
mano 'stitvaM pratyanyacca kAraNamucyate-tasmAnmano nAmAstayantaH karaNam, yasmAccakShuSho hyagocare pR^iShThapto 'pyupaspR^iShThaH kenicid hastasyAyaM sparsho jAnerayamiti vivekena pratipadyate /
yadi vivekakR^inmano nAma nAsti tarhi tvaÇmAtreNa kuto vivekapratipattiH syAt? tanmanaH /
asti tAvanmanaH, svarUpaM ca tasyApAdhigatam /
trINyannAnIha phalabhUtAni karmaNAM manovAkprANAkhyAni adhpAtmamadhibhUtamadhidaivaM ca vyAcikhyAsitAni /
tatra AdhyAtmikAnAM vAÇmanaH prANAnAM mano vyAkhyAtam /
athedArnIvAgvattkavyetyAraMmaH- yaH kashca loke shabdo dhavanistAlvAdivyaN^gyaH prANibhirvarNAdilakShaNa itaro vA vAditramedhAdinimittaH sarvo dhvanirvAgeva sA /
idaM tAvadvAcaH svarUpamuttkam? atha tasyAH kAryamucyate-eShA vAgghi yasmAdantamabhidheyAvasAnamabhidheyanirNayamAyattAnugatA /
eShA punaH svayaM nAbhidheyavatprakAshyA abhidheyaprakAshikaiv prakAshAtmakatvAt pradIpAdivat /
na hi pradIpAdiprakAshaH prakAshAntareNa prakAshyate, tadvadvAkprakAshikaiva svayaM na  prakAshyetyanavasthAM shrutiH pariharati - eShA hi na prakAshyA /
prakAshakatvameva vAcaH kAryamityarthaH /
atha prANa ucyate - prANo mukhanAsikAsaJNcAryA hR^idayavR^ittiHpraNayanAtprANaH apanayanAnmUtrapurIShAderapAnano 'dhovR^ittirAnAbhisthAnaH;vyAnano vyAyamanakarmA vyAnaH prANApAnayoH sandhirvIryavatkarmahetushca;udAna utkarShordhvagamanAdiheturApAdatalamastakasthAna UrdhvavR^ittiH, samAnaH samaM nayanAd bhuktasya pItasya ca koShThasthAno 'nnapaktA, ana ityeShAM vR^ittivisheShANAM sAmAnyabhUtA sAmAnyadehaceShTAbhisambandhinI vR^ittiH, evaM yathoktaM prANAdivR^ittijAtametatsarvaM prANa eva /
prANa ithi vR^ittimAnAdhyAtmiko 'na uktaH /
karma cAsya vR^ittibhedapradarshanenaiva vyAkhyAtam /
vyAkhyAtAnyAdhyAtmikAni manovAkprANAkhyAnyannAni /
etanmaya etadvikAraH prAjApatyairetairvAÇmanaH prANairArabdhaH /
ko 'sau? athaM kAryakaraNasaN^ghAta AtmA piNDa AtmasvarUpatvenAbhimato 'vivekibhiH /
avisheSheNaitanmaya ityuktasya visheSheNa vAÇmayo manomayaH prANamaya iti sphuTIkaraNam //3//

teShAmeva prAjApatyAnAmannAnAmAdhibhautiko vistAro 'bhidhIyate

#<trayo vedA eta eva |

#<devA pitaro manuShyA eta eva |

#<pitA mAtA prajaita eva |

START BrhUp 1,5.8

#<vij~nAtaM vijij~nAsyam avij~nAtam eta eva |
yat kiJNca vij~nAtaM vAcas tad rUpam |
vAg ghi vij~nAtA |
vAg enaM tad bhUtvAvati || BrhUp_1,5.8 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_1,5.8 vij~nAtaM vijij~nAsyamavij~nAtameta eva /
tatra visheShaH - yatkiJNca vij~nAtaM vispaShTaM j~nAtaM vAcastadrUpam /
tatra svayameva hetunAha - vAgdhi vij~nAtA prakAshAtmakatvAt /
kathamavij~nAtA bhaved yAnyAnapi vij~nApayadi"vAcaiva samrADbandhuH praj~nAyate"(4 / 1 / 2) iti hi vakShyati /
vAgvisheShavida idaM phalamucyate - vAgevainaM yathoktavAgvibhUtividaM tadvij~nAtaM bhUtvA avati pAlayati, vij~nAtarUpeNevAsyAnnaM bhojyatAM pratipadyata ityarthaH //8//



tathA -

START BrhUp 1,5.9

#<yat kiJNca vijij~nAsyaM manasas tad rUpam |
mano hi vijij~nAsyam |
mana enaM tad bhUtvAvati || BrhUp_1,5.9 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_1,5.9 yatkiJNca vijij~nAsyam, vispaShTaM j~nAtumiShTaM vijij~nAsyam, tatsarvaM manaso rUpam;mano hi yasmAsyam /
pUrvamanmanovibhUtividaH phalam - mana enaM tadvijij~nAsyaM bhUtvA avati vijij~nAsyasvarUpeNaivAnnatvamApadyate //9//



tathA -

START BrhUp 1,5.10

#<yat kiJNcAvij~nAtaM prANasya tad rUpam |
prANo hy avij~nAtaH |
prANa enaM tad bhUtvAvati || BrhUp_1,5.10 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_1,5.10 yatkiJNcAvij~nAtaM vij~nAnAgocaraM na ca sandihyamAnam, prANasya tadrUpam prANo hyavij~nAto 'niruktashruteH /
vij~nAtavijij~nAsyAvij~nAtabhedena vAÇmanaHprANavibhAge sthite trayo lokA ityAdayo vAcanikA eva /
sarvatra vij~nAtAdirUpadarshanAdvacanAdeva niyamaH smartavyaH /
prANa enaM tadbhUtvA avati - avij~nAtarUpeNaivAsya prANo 'nnaM bhavatItyarthaH /
shiShyaputrAdibhiH sandihyamAnAvij~nAtopakArA apyAcAryapitrAdayA dR^ishyante;tathA manaHprANayorapi sandihyamAnAvij~nAtayorannatvopapattiH //10//



vyAkhyAto vAÇmanaHprANAnAmAdhibhautiko vistAraH /
athAyamAdhidaivikArya ArambhaH -

START BrhUp 1,5.11

#<tasyai vAcaH pR^ithivI sharIram |
jyotIrUpam ayam agniH |
tad yAvaty eva vAk tAvatI pR^ithivI tAvAn ayam agniH || BrhUp_1,5.11 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_1,5.11 tasyai tasyAH vAcaH prajApaterannatvena prastutAyAH pR^ithivI sharIraM brahma AdhAraH, jyotIrUpaM prakAshAtmakaM karaNaM cAdheyaM prakAshaH, tadubhayaM pR^ithivyagni vAgeva prajApateH /
tattatra yAvatyeva yAvatparimANaiva adhyAtmAdhibhUtabhedabhinnA satI vAgbhavati, tatra sarvatra AdhAratvena pR^ithivI vyavasthitA, tAvatyeva bhavati kAryabhUtA;tAvAnayamagniH, AdheyaH karaNarUpo jyotirUpeNa pR^ithivImanupraviShTastAvAneva bhavati /
samAnamuttaram //11//

START BrhUp 1,5.12

#<athaitasya manaso dyauH sharIram |
jyotIrUpam asAv AdityaH |
tad yAvad eva manas tAvatI dyaus tAvAn asAv AdityaH |
tau mithunaM samaitAm |
tataH prANo 'jAyata |
sa indraH |
sa eSho 'sapatnaH |
dvitIyo vai sapatnaH |
nAsya sapatno bhavati ya evaM veda || BrhUp_1,5.12 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_1,5.12 athaitasya prAjApatyAnnoktasyaiva manaso dyaurdyulokaH sharIraM kAryamAdhAraH, jyotIrUpaM karaNamAdheyo 'sAvAdityaH /
tattatra yAvatparimANameva adhyAtmamadhibhUtaM vA manastAvatI tAvadvistArA tAvatparimANA manaso jyotIrUpasya karaNasya AdhAratvena vyavasthitA dyauH, tAvAnasAvAdityo jyotIrUpaM karaNamAdheyam /
tAvavagnyAdityau vAÇmanase Adhidaivike bhAtApitarau, mithunaM maithunyamitaretarasaMsarga samaitAM samagacchetAm /
'manasA Adityena prabhUtaM pitrA, vAcAgninA mAtrA prakAshitaM karma kariShyAmi'iti, antarA rodasyoH /
tatastayoreva saN^gamanAtprANo vAyuraj~nAyata parispandAya karmaNe /
yo jAtaH sa indraH parameshvaraH, na kevalamindra evAsapatno 'vidyamAnaH sapatno yasya;kaH punaH sapatnano nAma? dvitIyo vai pratipakShatvenopagataH sa dvitIyaH sapatna ityucyate /
tena dvitIyatve 'pi sati vAÇmanase na sapatnatvaM bhajete, prANaM prati guNabhAvopagate eva hi te adhyAtmamiva /
tatra prAsaN^gikAsapatnavij~nAnaphalamidam - nAsyaviduShaHsapatnaH pratipakSho bhavati, ya evaM yathoktaM prANamasapatnaM veda //12//




_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 1,5.13

#<athaitasya prANasyApaH sharIram |
jyotIrUpam asau candraH |
tad yAvAn eva prANas tAvatya Apas tAvAn asau candraH |
ta ete sarva eva samAH sarve 'nantAH |
sa yo haitAn antavata upAste 'ntavantaM sa lokaM jayati |
atha yo haitAn anantAn upAste 'nantaM sa lokaM jayati || BrhUp_1,5.13 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_1,5.13 athaitasya prakR^itasya prajApatyAnnasya prANamasya, na prajoktasyAntaranirdiShTasya, ApaH sharIraM kAryaM karaNAdhAraH, pUrvavajjayotIrUpamasau candraH /
tatrayAvaneva prANo yAvatparimANo 'dhyAtmAdibhedeShu, tAvadvyAptimatya ApaH tAvatparimANAH, tAvAnasau candro 'bAdheyastAsvapsvanupraviShTaH karaNabhUto 'dhyAtmamadhibhUtaM ca tAvadvyAptimAneva /
tAnyetAni pitrA pAN^ktena karmaNA sR^iShTAni trINyannAni vAÇmanaHprANAkhyAni /
adhyAtmamadhibhUtaM ca jagatsamastametairvyAptam, naitebhyo 'nyadatiriktaM kiJNcidasti kAryAtmakaM karaNAtmakaM vA /
samastAni tvetAni prajApatiH /
ta ete vAÇmanaHprANAH sarve eva samAstulyA vyAptimanto yAvatprANigocaraM sAdhyAtmAdhibhUtaM vyApya vyavasthitAH /
ata evAnantA yAvatsaMsArabhAvinano hi te /
na hi kAryakaraNapratyAkhyAnena saMsAro 'vagamyate /
kAryakaraNAtmakA hi ta ityuktam /
sa yaH kashcid haitAnprajApaterAtmabhUtAnantavataHparicchinnAnadhyAtmarUpeNa vA adhibhUtarUpeNa vA adhibhUtarUpeNa vopAste, sa ca tadupAsanAnurUpameva phalamantavantaM lokaM jayati, paricchinna eva jAyate naiteShAmAtmabhUto bhavatItyarthaH /
atha punaryo haitAnanantAnsarvAtmakAnsarvaprANyAtmabhUtAn aparicchinnAnupAste so 'ntameva lokaM jayati //13//



pitA pAN^ktena karmaNA saptAnnAni sR^iShTvA trINyannAnyAtmArthaN^karodityuktam /
tAnyetAni /
pAN^ktakarmaphalabhUtAni vyAkhyAtAni /
tatra kathaM punaH pAN^ktatAvagamyate, vittakarmaNamorapi tatra sambhavAt /
tatra pR^ithivyagnI mAtA, divAdityau pitA /
yo 'pyamanayorantarA prANaH, sa prajeti vyAkhyAtam /
tatra vittakarmaNI sambhAvayitavye ityArambhaH -

START BrhUp 1,5.14

#<sa eSha saMvatsaraH prajApatiSh ShoDashakalaH |
tasya rAtraya eva paJNcadasha kalA |
dhruvaivAsya ShoDashI kalA |
sa rAtribhir evA ca pUryate 'pa ca kShIyate |
so 'mAvAsyAM rAtrim etayA ShoDashyA kalayA sarvam idaM prANabhR^id anupravishya tataH prAtar jAyate |
tasmAd etAM rAtriM prANabhR^itaH prANaM na vicchindyAd api kR^ikalAsasyaitasyA eva devatAyA apacityai || BrhUp_1,5.14 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_1,5.14 'sa eShaH saMvatsaraH' -yo 'yaM tryannAtmA prajApatiH prakR^itaH, sa eSha saMvatsarAtmanA visheShato nirdishyate /
ShoDashakalaH ShoDasha kalA avayavA asya so 'yaM ShoDashakalaH saMvatsaraH saMvatsarAtmAkAlarUpaH /
tasya ca kAlAtmanaH prajApateH rAtraya evAhorAtrANi, tithaya ityarthaH, paJNcadasha kalAH /
dhruvaiva nityaiva vyavasthitA asya prajApateH ShoDashI ShoDashAnAM pUraNI kalA /
sa rAtribhireva tithibhiH kaloktAbhirApUryate cApakShIyate ca /
pratipadAdyAbhirhi candramAH prajApatiH shuklapakSha ApUryate kalAbhirupacIyamAnAbhirvardhate yAvatsampUrNamaNDalaH paurNamAsyAm /
tAbhirevApacIyamAnAbhiH kalAbhirapakShIyate kR^iShNapakShe yAvad dhruvaikA kalA vyavasthitA amAvAsyAm /
sa prajApatiH kalAtmA amAvAsyAmamAvAsyAyAM rAtriMrAtrau yA vyavasthitA dhruvA kaloktA etayA ShoDashyA kalayA sarvamidaM prANabhR^itprANijAtamanupravishya yadapaH pibati yaccaupadhIrashnAti tatsarvameva oShadhyAtmanA sarvaM vyApyAmAvAsyAM rAtrimavasthAya tato 'paredyuH prAtarj~nAyate dvitIyayA kalayA saMyuktaH /
evaM pAN^ktAtmako 'sau prajApatiH /
divAdityau manaH pitA;pR^ithivyagno vAgj~nAyA mAtA;tayoshca prANaH prajA /
cAndramasyastithayaH kalA vittam, upacayApacayadharmitvAdvittavat /
tAsAM ca kalAnAM kAlAvayavAnAM jagatpariNAmahetutvaM karma /
evameSha kR^itsnaH prajApatiH"jAyA me syAdatha prajAyeyAtha vittaM me syAdatha karma kurvIya" (bR^i.u.1 / 4 / 17) ityeShaNAnurUpa eva pAN^ktasya karmaNaH phalabhUtaH saMvR^ittaH /
kAraNAnuvidhAyi hi kAryamiti loke 'pi sthitiH /
yasmAdeSha candra etAM rAtriM sarvaprANijAtamanupraviShTo dhruvayA kalayA vartate, tasmAddhetoretAmamAvAsyAM rAtriM prANabhR^itaH prANinaH prANaM na vicchindyAtprANinaM na pramApayedityetat, api kR^ikalAsasya /
kR^ikalAso hi pApAtmA svabhAvenaiva hiMsyate prANibhirdR^iShTo 'pyamaN^gala iti kR^itvA /
bADhaM pratiShiddhA, tathApi nAmAvAsyAyA anyatra pratiprasavArthaM vacanaM hiMsAyAH kR^ikalAsaviShaye vA, kiM tarhi? etasyAH somadevatAyA apacityai pUjArtham //14//




_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 1,5.15

#<yo vai sa saMvatsaraH prajApatiH ShoDashakAlo 'yam eva sa yo 'yam evaMvit puruShaH |
tasya vittam eva paJNcadasha kalAH |
AtmaivAsya ShoDashI kalA |
sa vittenaivA ca pUryate 'pa ca kShIyate |
tad etan nabhyaM yad ayam AtmA |
pradhir vittam |
tasmAd yady api sarvajyAniM jIyata AtmanA cej jIvati pradhinAgAd ity evAhuH || BrhUp_1,5.15 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_1,5.15 yo vai parokShAbhihitaH saMvatsaraH prajApatiH ShoDashakalaH sa naivAtyantaM parokSho mantavyaH, yasmAdayameva sa pratyakSha upalabhyate /
ko 'sAvayam? yo yathektaM tryannAtmakaM prajApatimAtmabhUtaM vetti sa evaMvitpuruShaH /
kena sAmAnyena prajApatiriti taducyate - tasyaivaMvidaH puruShasya gavAdi vittameva paJNcadasha kalA upacayApacayadharmitvAt;tadvittasAdhyaM ca karma /
tasya kR^itsnatAyai Atmaiva piNDa evAsya viduShaH ShoDashI kalA dhruvasthAnIyA /
sa candravadvittenaivApUryate cApakShIyate ca - tadetalloke prasiddham /
tadetannabhyam, nAbhyai hitaM nabhyaM nAbhiM vA arhatIti /
kiM tat? yadayaM yo 'yamAtmA piNDaH /
pradhirvittaM parivArasthAnIyaM bAhyaM cakrasyevAranemyAdi /
tasmAdyadyapi sarvajyAniM sarvasvApaharaNaM jIyate hIyate glAniM prApnoti, AtmanA cakranAbhisthAnIyena cedyadi jIvati pradhinA bAhyena parivAreNAyamagAtkShINo 'yaM yathA cakramaranemivimuktamevamAhuH /
jIvaMshced aranemisthAnIyena vittena punarupacIyata ityabhiprAyaH //15//



evaM pAN^ktena daivavittavidyAsaMyuktena karmaNA tryannAtmakaH prajApatirbhavatIti vyAkhyAtam /
anantaraM ca jAyAdivittaM parivArasthAnIyamityuktam /
tatra putrakarmAparavidyAnAM lokaprAptisAdhanatvamAtraM sAmAnyenAvagatam, na putrAdInA lokaprAptiphalaM prati visheShasambandhaniyamaH /
so 'yaM putrAdInAM sAdhanAnAM sAdhyavisheShasambandho vaktavya ityuttarakaNDikA praNIyate -




_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 1,5.16

#<atha trayo vAva lokA manuShyalokaH pitR^iloko devaloka iti |
so 'yaM manuShyalokaH putreNaiva jayyo nAnyena karmaNA |
karmaNA pitR^ilokaH |
vidyayA devalokaH |
devaloko vai lokAnAM shreShThaH |
tasmAd vidyAM prashaMsanti || BrhUp_1,5.16 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_1,5.16 atheti vAkyopanyAsArthaH /
trayaH, vAvetyavadhAraNArthaH /
traya eva shAstroktasAdhanArhA lokAH, na nyUnA nAdhikA vA /
ke te? ityucyate - manuShyalokaH pitR^iloko deloka iti /
teShAM so 'yaM manuShyalokaH putreNaiva sAdhanena jayyo jetavyaH sAdhyaH - yathA ca putreNa jetavyastathottaratra vakShyAmaH, - nAnyena karmaNA, vidyayA veti vAkyasheShaH /
karmaNA agnihotrAdilakShaNena kevalena pitR^iloko jetavyo na putreNa nApi vidyayA /
vidyayA devaloko na putreNa nApi karmaNA /
devaloko vai lokAnAM trayANAM shreShThaH prashasyatamaH /
tasmAttatsAdhanatvAdvidyAM prashaMsanti //16//



evaM sAdhyalokatrayaphalabhedena viniyuktAni putrakarmavidyAkhyAni trINi sAdhanAni /
jAyA tu putrakarmArthatvAnna pR^ithaksAdhanamiti pR^ithaÇnAbhihitA /
vittaM ca karmasAdhanatvAnna pR^ithaksAdhanam /
vidyAkarmaNorlokajayahetutvaM svAtmapratilAbhenaiva bhavatIti prasiddham /
putrasya tvakriyAtmakatvAtkena prakAreNa lokajayahetutvamiti na j~nAyate /
atastadvaktavyamityathAnantaramArabhyate -

START BrhUp 1,5.17

#<athAtaH samprattiH |
yadA praiShyan manyate 'tha putram Aha -- tvaM brahma tvaM yaj~nas tvaM loka iti |
sa putraH pratyAhAhaM brahmAhaM yaj~no 'ham loka iti |
yad vai kiJNcAnUktaM tasya sarvasya brahmety ekatA |
ye vai ke ca yaj~nAs teShAM sarveShAM yaj~na ity ekatA |
ye vai ke ca lokAs teShAM sarveShAM loka ity ekatA |
etAvad vA idaM sarvam |
etan mA sarvaM sann ayam ito bhunajad iti |
tasmAt putram anushiShTaM lokyam AhuH |
tasmAd enam anushAsati |
sa yadaivaMvid asmAl lokAt praity athaibhir eva prANaiH saha putram Avishati |
sa yady anena kiJNcid akShNayA kR^itaM bhavati tasmAd enaM sarvasmAt putro muJNcati tasmAt putro nAma |
sa putreNaivAsmil loke pratitiShThati |
athainam ete devAH prANA amR^itA Avishanti || BrhUp_1,5.17 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_1,5.17 sampratiH sampradAnam;samprattiriti vakShyamANasya karmaNo nAmadheyam /
putro hi svAtmavyApArasampradAnaM karotyanena prakAreNa pitA, tena samprattisaMj~nakamidaM karma /
tatkasminkAle kartavyam? ityAha - sa pitA yadA yasmin kAle praiShyan mariShyan mariShyAmItyapariShTAdidarshanena manyate, atha tadA putramAhUyAha - tvaM brahma tvaM yaj~nastvaM loka iti /
sa evamuktaH putraH pratyAha;sa tu pUrvamevAnushiShTo jAnAti mayaitatkartavyamiti, tenAha - ahaM brahmAhaM yaj~no 'haM loka ithi /
etadvAkyatrayam /
etasyArthastirohita iti manvAnA shrutirvyAkhyAnAya pravartate /
yadvai kiJNca yatkiJNcAvashiShTamanUktamadhItamanadhItaM ca, tasya sarvasyaiva brahmetyetasminpade ekatA ekatvam yo 'dhyayanavyApAro mama kartavya AsIdetAvantaM kAlaM vedaviShayaH, sa ita UrdhvaM tvaM brahma tvatkartR^iko 'stvityarthaH /
tathA ye vai ke ca yaj~nA anuShTheyAH santo mayA anuShThitAshcAnanuShThitAshca, teShAM sarveShAM yaj~na ityetasminpade ekataikatvam, matkartR^ikA yaj~nA ya Asan, te ita UrdhvaM tvaM yaj~naH - tvatkartR^ikA bhavantvityarthaH /
ye vai ke ca lokA mayA jetavyAH santo jitA ajitAshca, teShAM sarveShAM loka ityetasminpade ekatA /
ita UrdhvaM mayAdhyayanayaj~nalokajayakartavyakratustvayi samarpitaH, ahaM tu mukto 'smi kartavyatAbandhanaviShayAtkratoH /
sa ca sarvaM tathaiva pratipannavAnputro 'nushiShTatvAt /
tatremaM piturabhiprAyaM manvAnA AcaShTa shrutiH - etAvadetatparimANaM vai idaM sarvaM yadgR^ihiNA kartavyam, yaduta vedA adhyetavyAH, yaj~nA yaShTavyAH, lokAshca jetavyAH /
etanmA sarvaM sannayam - sarvaM hImaM bhAraM madadhInaM matto 'pacchidya Atamani nidhAya, ito 'smAllokAnmA mAm abhunajatpAlayiShyatIti /
ÊDarthe laÇ, chandasi kAlaniyamAbhAvAt /
yasmAdevaM sampannaH putraH pitaram asmAllokAtkartavyatAbandhanato mocayiShyati, tasmAtputramanushiShTaM lokyaM lokahitaM piturAhurbrAhmaNAH /
ata eva hyenaM putramanushAsati, lokyo 'yaM naH syAditi, pitaraH /
sa pitA yadA yasminkAle evaMvitputrasamarpitakartavyatAkratuH, asmAllokAtpaiti mriyate, atha tadaibhireva prakR^itairvAÇmanaHprANaiH putramAvishati putraM vyApnoti /
adhyAtmaparicchedahetvapagamAt piturvAÇmanaHprANAHsvena Adhidaivikena rUpeNa pR^ithivyagnyAdyAtmanA bhinnaghaTapradIpaprakAshavatsarvamAvishanti /
taiH prANaiH saha pitAtyAvishati, vAÇmanaHprANAtmabhAvitvAtpituH /
ahamasmyanantA vAÇmanaHprANA adhyAtmAdibhedavistArA ityevaM bhAvito hi pitA /
tasmAttatprANAnuvR^ittitvaM piturbhavatIti yuktamuktam - ebhireva prANaiH saha putramAvishatIt;sarveShAM hyasAvAtmA bhavati putrasya ca /
etaduktaM bhavati - yasya piturevamanushiShTaH putro bhavati so 'sminneva loke vartate putrarUpeNa, naiva mR^ito mantavya ityarthaH /
tathA ca shrutyantare -"so 'syAyamitara AtmA puNyebhyaH karmabhyaH pratidhIyate"(ai.u.4 / 4) iti /
athedAnIM putranirvacanamAha - sa putro yadi kadAcidanena pitrA akShNyA koNacchidrato 'ntarA akR^itaM bhavati kartavyam, tasmAt, kartavyatArUpAtpitrA akR^itAt sarvasmAllokaprAptipratibandharUpAtputro muJNcati mocayati tatsarvaM svayamanutiShThanpUrayitvA /
tasmAtpUraNena trAyate sa pitaraM yasmAttasmAtputro nAma /
idaM tatputrasya putratvaM yatpitushchidraM pUrayitvA trAyate /
sa pitaivaMvidhena putreNa mR^ito 'pi sannamR^ito 'sminneva loke pratitiShThati, evamasau pitA putreNemaM manuShyalokaM jayati /
na tathA vidyAkarmabhyAM devalokapitR^ilokau svarUpalAbhasattAmAtreNa;na hi vidyAkarmaNI svarUpalAbhavyatirekeNa putravadvyApArAntarApekShayA lokajayahetutvaM pratipadyete /
atha kR^itasamprattikaM pitaramenamete vAgAdayaH prANA daivA hairaNyagarbhA amR^itA amaraNadharmANa Avishanti kathamiti vakShyati pR^ithivyai cainamityAdi /
evaM putrakarmAparavidyAnAM manuShyalokapitR^ilokadeva lokasAdhyArthatA pradarshitA shrutyA svayameva /
atra kecidvAvadUktAH shrutyuktavisheShaviniyogopasahAreNa ca /
tasmAdR^iNashrutiravidvadviShayA na paramAtmavidviShayeti siddham /
vakShyati ca  -"kariShyAmo yeShAM no 'yamAtmAyaM lokaH" (4 / 4 / 22) iti /
kecittu pitR^ilokadevalokajayo 'pi pitR^ilokadevalokAbhyAM vyAvR^ittireva;tasmAtputrakarmAparavidyAbhiH samucityAnuShThitAbhistribhya etebhyo lokebhyo vyAvR^ittaH paramAtmavij~nAnena mokShamadhigacchatIti paramparayA mokShArthAnyeva putrAdisAdhanAnIcchanti /
teShAmapi mukhApidhAnAyeyameva shrutiruttarA kR^itasamprattikasya putriNaH karmiNaH tryannAtmavidyAvidaH, phalapradarshanAya pravR^ittA /
na cedameva phalaM mokShaphalamiti shakyaM, vaktum, tryannasambandhAt, medhAtapaHkAryatvAccAnnAnAm,'punaH punarjanayate'iti darshanAt; 'yaddhaitanna kuryAtkShIyeta ha'iti ca kShayashravaNAt /
sharIraM jyotIrUpamiti ca kAryakaraNatvopapatteH /
'trayaM vA idam'iti ca nAmarUpakarmAtmakatvenopasaMhArAt /
na cedameva sAdhanatrayaM saMhataM satkasyacinmokShArthaM kasyacit tryannAtmaphalamityasmAdeva vAkyAdavagantu  shakyam, putrAdisAdhanAnAM tryannAtmaphaladarshanenaivopakShINatvAd vAkyasya /

START BrhUp 1,5.18

#<pR^ithivyai cainam agnesh ca daivI vAg Avishati |

BrhUpBh_1,5.18 pR^ithivyai pR^ithivyAH ca enam agneshca daivI adhidaivAtmikA vAgenaM kR^itasamprattikamAvishati /

START BrhUp 1,5.20

#<adbhyash cainaM candramasash ca daivaH prANa Avishati |
sa vai daivaH prANo yaH saMcaraMsh cAsaMcaraMsh ca na vyathate 'tho na riShyati |
sa eSha evaMvit sarveShAM bhUtAnAm AtmA bhavati |
yathaiShA devataivaM saH |
yathaitAM devatAM sarvANi bhUtAny avanty evaM haivaMvidaM sarvANi bhUtAny avanti |
yad u kiJNcemAH prajAH shocanty amaivAsAM tad bhavati |
puNyam evAmuM gacchati |
na ha vai devAn pApaM gacchati || BrhUp_1,5.20 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_1,5.20 adbhayashcainaM candramasashca daivaH prANa Avishati /
sa vai daivaH prANaH kiMllakShaNaH? ityucyate-yaH saJNcaran prANibhedeShva saJNcaransamaShTivya ShTirUpeNa--athavA saJNcarana jaN^gameShu asaJNcaransthAvareShu, na vyathate na duHkhanimittena bhayena yuDyate /
athAM api na riShyati na vinashyati na hiMsAmApadyate /
saH--yo yathoktamevaM vetti vyannAtmadarshanaM saH-sarveShAM bhUtAnAM prANo bhavati, sarveShAM bhUtAnAM mano bhavati, sarveShAM bhUtAnAM vAgbhavati-ityevaM sarvAbhUtAtmatayA sarvaj~no bhavatItyarthaH;sarvakR^icca /
tathaipA pUrvasidvA hiraNyagarbhadevatA evameva nAsya sarvaj~natve sarvakR^ittave vA kkacitpratighAtaH /
sa iti dArShTAntikanirdeshaH /
kiJNca yathaitAMd diraNyagarbhadevatAmijyAdibhiH sarvANi bhUtAnyavanti pAlayanti pUjyanti, evaM ha evaMvidaM sarvANi bhUtAnyavanti-ijyAdilakShaNAM pUjAM satataM prayapaJNjata ityarthaH /
athedamAshaN^kayate-sarvaprANinAmAtmA bhavatItyuttkam, tasya ca sarvaprANikAryakaraNAtmatve sarvaprANisukhaduHkhaiH sambadhyeteti /
tanna, aparicchinnabudvitvAt paricchinnAtmabudvInAM hyAkroshAdau duHkhasambandho dR^iShTaH- anenAhamAkruShTa iti /
asya tu sarvAtmano ya Akrushyate yashcAkroshati yatorAtmatvabudvivisheShAbhAvAnna tannimittaM duHkhamupapadyate /
maraNaduHkhavacca nimittAbhAvAt yathA hi kasmiMshcinmR^ite kasyacid duHkhamutpadyate-mamAsauputrobhrAtAceti, putrAdinimittam;tannimittAbhAve tanmaraNadarshino 'pi naiva duHkhamupajAyate, tatheshvarasyApyaparicchinnAtmano mamatavatAdiduHkhanimittamidhyAj~nAnAdidopAbhAvAnnaiva duHkhamupajAyate /
tadetaducyate-yadu kiJNcayat kiJNca imAH prajAH shocantyamaiva sahaiva prajAbhistacchokAdinimittaM duHkhaM saMyuktaM bhavatyAsAM prajAnAM paricchinnabudvijanitatvAt /
sarvAtmanastu kena saha kiM saMyukta bhavedviyukta vA? amuM tu prAjApatye pade vartamAnaM puNyameva shubhamevaphalamabhipretaM puNyamiti-niratishayaM hi tena puNyaM kR^itam;tena tatphalameva gacchati /
na ha vai devAnpApaM gacchati, pApaphalasyAvasarAbhAvAt pApaphalaM duHkha na gacchatItyathaH //20//



'ta ete sarva eva samAH sarve 'nantAH'ityavisheSheNa vAÇmanaHprANAnAmupAsanamuktam, nAnyatamagato vesheSha uktaH /
kimevameva pratipattavyam? kiM vA vicAryamANe kashcidvisheSho vratamupAsanaM prati pratitapattuM shakyate? ityucyate-

START BrhUp 1,5.21

#<athAto vratamImAMsA |
prajApatir ha karmANi sasR^ije |
tAni sR^iShTAny anyo 'nyenAspardhanta |
vadiShyAmy evAham iti vAg dadhre |
drakShyAmy aham iti cakShuH |
shroShyAmy aham iti shrotram |
evam anyAni karmANi yathAkarmam |
tAni mR^ityuH shramo bhUtvopayeme |
tAny Apnot |
tAny AptvA mR^ityur avArundha |

shrAmyati shrotram |
athemam eva nApnot yo 'yaM madhyamaH prANaH |
tAni j~nAtuM dadhrire |
ayaM vai naH shreShTho yaH saMcaraMsh cAsaMcaraMsh ca na vyathate 'tho na riShyati |
hantAsyaiva sarve rUpaM bhavAmeti |
ta etasyaiva sarve rUpam abhavan |
tasmAd eta etenAkhyAyante prANA iti |
tena ha vAva tat kulam AcakShate yasmin kule bhavati ya evaM veda |
ya u haivaMvidA spardhate 'nushuShyati |
anushuShya haivAntato mriyata ity adhyAtmam || BrhUp_1,5.21 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_1,5.21 athAto 'nantaraM vratamImAMsA upAsanakarmavicAraNetyarthaH /
eShAM prANAnAM kasya karma vratatvena dhArayitavyamiti mImAMsA pravartate /
tatra prajApatirha - hashabdaH kilArthe - prajApatiH kila prajAH sR^iShTvA karmANi karaNAni vAgAdIni - karmAthAni hi tAnIti karmANItyucyante - sasR^ije sR^iShTavAnvAgAdIni karaNAnItyarthaH /
tAni punaH sR^iShTAnyanyonyena itaretaramaspardhanta spardhAM saMgharShaM cakruH /
katham? vadiShyAmyeva svavyApArAdvadanAdanuparataivAhaM syAmiti vAgvrataM dadhre dhR^itavatI - yadyanyo 'pi matsamo 'sti svavyApArAdanuparantuM shaktaH, so 'pi darshayatvAtmano vIryamiti /
tathA drakShyAmyahamiti cakShuH, shroShyAmyahamiti shrotram;evamanyAni karmANi karaNAni yathAkarma - yadyadyasya karma yathAkarma /
tAni karaNAni mR^ityurmArakaH shramaH shramarUpI bhUtvA upayeme saJNjagrAha /
katham? tAni karaNAni svavyApAre pravR^ittAnyApnot, shramarUpeNAtmAnaM darshitavAn /
AptvA ca tAnyavArundha avarodhaM kR^itavAnmR^ityuH - svakarmabhyaH pracyAvitavAnityarthaH /
tasmAdadyatve 'pi vadane svakarmaNi pravR^ittA vAk shrAmyatvena shramarUpiNA mR^ityunA saMyuktA svakarmataH pracyavate /
tathA shrAmyati cakShuH, shrAmyati shrotram /
athemameva mukhyaM prANaM nApnonna prAptavAnmR^ityuH shramarUpI, yo 'yaM madhyamaH prANastam /
tenAdyatve 'pyashrAnta eva svakarmaNi pravartate /
tAnItarANi karaNAni taM j~nAtuM dadhrire dhR^itavanti manaH /
ayaM vai no 'smAkaM madhye shreShThaH prashasyatamo 'bhyadhikaH, yasmAdyaH saJNcaraMshcAsaJNcaraMshca na vyathate 'tho na riShyati - hantedAnImasyaiva prANasya sarve vayaM rUpamasAma prANamAtmatvena pratipadyemahi - evaM vinishcitya te etasyaiva sarve rUpamabhavan;prANarUpamevAtmatvena pratipannAH, prANavratameva dadhrire - asmadvratAni na mR^ityorvAraNAya paryAptAnIti /
yasmAtprANena rUpeNa rUpavantItarANi karaNAni calanAtmanA svena ca prakAshAtmanaH, na hi prANAdanyatra calanAtmakatvopapattiH;calanavyApArapUrvakANyeva hi sarvadA svavyApAreShu lakShyante;tasmAdete vAgAdaya etena prANAbhidhAnena AkhyAyante 'bhidhIyante prANA ityevam /
ya evaM prANAtmatAM sarvakaraNAnAM vetti prANashabdAbhidheyatvaM ca, tena ha vAva tenaiva viduShA tatkulamAcakShate laukikAH /
yasminkule sa vidvAJNjAto bhavati tatkulaM vidvAJNjAto bhavati tatkulaM vidvannAmnaiva prathitaM bhavatyamuShyadaM kulamiti, yathA tApatya iti /
ya evaM yathoktaM veda vAgAdInAM prANarUpatAM prANAkhyatvaM ca tasyaitatphalam /
kiJNca yaH kashcidu haivaMvidA prANAtmadarshinA spardhate tatpratipakShI san, so 'sminneva sharIre 'nushuShyati shoShamupagacchati /
anushuShya haiva shoShaM gatvaiva antato 'nte mriyate na sahasAnupadruto mriyate ityaivamuktamadhyAtmaM prANAtmadarshanamityuktopasaMhAro 'dhidaivatapradarshanArthaH //21//

START BrhUp 1,5.22

#<athAdhidevataM:
jvaliShyAmy evAham ity agnir dadhre |
tapsyAmy aham ity AdityaH |
bhAsyAmy aham iti candramAH |
evam anyA devatA yathAdevatam |
sa yathaiShAM prANAnAM madhyamaH prANa evam etAsAM devatAnAM vAyuH |

BrhUpBh_1,5.22 athAnantaram adhidaivataM devatAviShayaM darshanamucyate /

mlocantyastaM yanti svakarmebhya uparamante - yathAdhyAtmaM vAgAdayo 'nyA devatA agnyAdyAH, na vAyurastaM yAti - yathA madhyamaH prANaH, ataH saiShA anastamitA devatA yadvAyuryo 'yaM vAyuH /

START BrhUp 1,5.23

#<athaiSha shloko bhavati --
yatash codeti sUryo 'staM yatra ca gacchatIti |
prANAd vA eSha udeti prANe 'stam eti |
taM devAsh cakrire dharmaM sa evAdya sa u shva iti |
yad vA ete 'murhy adhriyanta tad evApy adya kurvanti |
tasmAd ekam eva vrataM caret prANyAc caivApAnyAc ca |
nen mA pApmA mR^ityur Apnavad iti |
yady u caret samApipayiShet teno etasyai devatAyai sAyujyaM salokatAM jayati || BrhUp_1,5.23 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_1,5.23 athaitasyaivArthasya prakAshaka eSha shloko mantro bhavati /
yatashca yasmAdvAyorudetyudgacchati sUryaH, adhyAtmaM ca cakShurAtmanA prANAd astaM ca yatra vAyau prANe ca gacchatyaparasaMdhyAsamaye svApasamaye ca puruShasya, taM devAstaM dharmaM devAshcakrire dhR^itavanto vAgAdayo 'gnyAdayashca prANavrataM ca purA vicArya /
sa evAdyedAnIM shvo 'pi bhaviShyatyapi kAle 'nuvartyate 'nuvartiShyate ca devairityabhiprAyaH /
tatremaM mantraM saMkShepato vyAcaShTa brAhmaNam - prANAdvA eSha sUrya udeti prANe 'stameti /
taM devAshcakrire dharmaM sa evAdya sa u shva ityasya kor'thaH? ityucyate - yadvai ete vratamamurhi amuShminkAle vAgAdayo 'gnyAdayashca prANavrataM vAyuvrataM cAdhriyanta, tadevAdyApi kurvantyanuvartate 'nuvartiShyante ca /
vrataM tairabhagnameva /
yattu vAgAdivratamagnyAdivrataM ca tadbhagnameva, teShAmastamanakAle svApakAle ca vAyau prANe ca nimsuktidarshanAt /
athaitadanyatroktam"yadA vai puraShaH svapiti prANaM tarhi vAgapyeti prANaM manaH prANaM cakShuHprANaM shrotraM yadA prabudhyate prANAdevAdhi punarjAyanta ityadhyAtmamathAdhidaivataM yadA vA agniranugacchati vAyuM tarhyanUdvAti yadAdityo 'stameti vAyuM tarhi pravishati vAyuM candramA vAyau dishaH pratiShThitA vAyorevAdhi punarjAyante"iti /
yasmAde etadeva vrataM vAgAdiShvagnyAdiShu cAnugataM yadetadvAyoshca prANasya ca parispandAtmakatvaM sarvedevairuvartyamAnaM vratam tasmAdanyo 'pyokameva vrataM caret /
kiM tata? prANyAtprANanavyApAraM kuryAdapAnyAdapAnanadhyApAraM ca;na hi prANApAnavyApArasya prANanApAnanalakShaNasyoparamo 'sti /
tasmAttadevaikaM vrataM careddhitvendriyAntaravyApAraM nenmA mAM pApmA mR^ityuH shramarUpyApnuvadApnuyAt /
necchabdaH paribhaye -'yadyahamasmAd vratAtpracyutaH syAm, grasta evAhaM mR^ityunA'ityevaM trasto dhArayetprANavratamityabhiprAyaH /
yadi kadAcid u caretprArabheta prANavratam, samApipayiShetsamApayitumicchet;yadi hyasmAd vratAduparametprANaH paribhUtaH syAddevAshca;tasmAtsamApayedeva /
tena u tenAnena vratena prANAtmapratipattyA sarvabhUteShu - vAgAdayo 'gnyAdayashca madAtmakA eva, ahaM prANa AtmA sarvaparispandakR^it - evaM tenAnena vratadhAraNena etasyA eva prANadevatAyAH sAyujyaM sayugbhAvamekAtmatvaM salokatAM samAnalokatAM vA ekasthAnatvam - vij~nAnamAndyopekShametat - jayati prApnotIt //23//

#<iti bR^ihadAraNyakopaniShadbhAShye prathamAdhyAye paJNcamaM saptAnnabrahmaNam //5//>#



yadetadavidyAviShayatvena prastutaM sAdhyasAdhanalakShaNaM vyAkR^itaM jagat prANAtmaprAptyantotkarShavadapi phalam, yA caitasya vyAkaraNAtprAgavasthA avyAkR^itashabdavAcyA vR^ikShabIjavatsarvametat /

START BrhUp 1,6.1

#<trayaM vA idaM nAma rUpaM karma |
teShAM nAmnAM vAg ity etad eShAm uktham |
ato hi sarvANi nAmAny uttiShThanti |
etad eShAM sAma |
etad dhi sarvair nAmabhiH samam |
etad eShAM brahma |
etad dhi sarvANi nAmAni bibharti || BrhUp_1,6.1 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_1,6.1 trayam;kiM tattrayam? ityucyate /
nAma rUpaM karma cetyanAtmaiva /
nAtmA yatsAkShAdaparokShAdbrahma /
tasmAdasmAdvirajyetetyevamarthastrayaM vA ityAdyArambhaH na hyasmAdanAtmano 'vyAvR^itticittasya AtmAnameva lokamahaM brahmAsmItyupAsituM buddhiH pravartate /
bAhyapratyagAtmapravR^ittyorvirodhAt /
tathA ca kAThake -"parAJNci khAni vyatR^iNatsvayambhUstasmAtparAÇpashyati nAntarAtman /
kashciddhIraH pratyagAtmAnamaikShadAvR^ittacakShuramR^itatvamicchan" (ka.u.2 / 1 / 1) ityAdi /
kathaM punarasya vyAkR^itAvyAkR^itasya kriyAkArakaphalAtmanaH saMsArasya nAmarUpakarmAtmakataiva? na punarAtmatvam? ityetatsambhAvayituM shakyata iti;atrocyate - teShAM nAmnAM yathopanyastAnAM vAgiti shabdasAmAnyamucyate /
"yaH kashca shabdo vAgeva sA"(1 / 5 / 3) ityuktatvAdvAdityetasya shabdasya yor'thaH shabdasya shabdasAmAnyamAtram etadeteShAM nAmavisheShANAmukthaM kAraNamupAdAnam, saindhavalavaNakaNAnAmiva saindhavAcalaH /
tadAha - ato hyasmAnnAmasAmAnyAtsarvANi nAmAni yaj~nadatto devadatta ityevamAdipravibhAgAnyuttiShThantyutpadyante pravibhajyante, lavaNAcalAdiva lavaNakaNAH;kAryaM ca kAraNenAvyatiriktam /
tathA visheShANAM ca sAmAnye 'ntarbhAvAt /
kathaM sAmAnyavisheShabhAva iti etacchabda sAmAnyameShAM nAmavisheShANAM sAma /
samatvAtsAma, sAmAnyamityarthaH, etaddhi yasmAtsarvairnAmabhirAtmavisheShaiH samam /
kiJNca AtmalAbhAvisheShAcca nAmavisheShANAm /
yasya ca yasmAdAtmalAbho bhavati sa tenApravibhakto dR^iShTaH, yathA ghaTAdInAM mR^idA /
kathaM nAmavisheShANAmAtmalAbho vAca ityucyate yata etadeShAM vAkchabdavAcyaM vastu brahma AtmA, tato hyAtmalAbho nAmnAm, shabdavyatiriktasvarUpAnupapatteH /
tatpratipAdayati - yatashchabdasAmAnyaM hi yasmAcchabdavisheShAnsarvANi nAmAni bibharti dhArayati svarUpapradAnena /
evaM kAryakAraNatvopapatteH sAmAnyavisheShopapatterAtmapradAnopapattashca nAmavisheShANAM shabdamAtratA siddhA /
evamuttarayorapi sarvaM yojyaM yathoktam //1//

START BrhUp 1,6.2

#<atha rUpANAM cakShur ity etad eShAm uktham |
ato hi sarvANi rUpANy uttiShThanti |
etad eShAM sAma |
etad dhi sarvai rUpaiH samam |
etad eShAM brahma |
etad dhi sarvANi rUpANi bibharti || BrhUp_1,6.2 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_1,6.2 athedAnIM rUpANAM sitAsitaprabhR^itInAM cakShuriti cakShurviShayasAmAnyaM cakShuHshabdAbhidheyaM rUpasAmAnyaM prakAshyamAtramabhidhIyate /
ato hi sarvANi rUpANyittiShThanti, etadeShAM sAma, etaddhi sarvai rUpeH samam, etadeShAM brahma, etaddhi sarvANi rUpANi bibharti //2//




_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 1,6.3

#<atha karmaNAm Atmety etad eShAm uktham |
ato hi sarvANi karmANy uttiShThanti |
etad eShAM sAma |
etad dhi sarvaiH karmabhiH samam |
etad eShAM brahma |
etad dhi sarvANi karmANi bibharti |
tad etat trayaM sad ekam ayam AtmA |
Atmo ekaH sann etat trayam |
tad etad amR^itaM satyena channam |
prANo vA amR^itam |
nAmarUpe satyam |
tAbhyAm ayaM prANash channaH || BrhUp_1,6.3 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_1,6.3 athedAnIM sarvakarmavisheShANAM mananadarshanAtmakAnAM calanAtmakAnAM ca kriyAsAmAnyamAtre 'ntarbhAva ucyate /
katham? sarveShaM karmavisheShANAmAtmA sharIraM sAmAnyamAtmA, AtmanaH karma Atmetyucyate /
'AtmanA hi sharIreNa karma karoti'ityuktam /
sharIre ca sarvaM karmAbhivyajyat /
ataH tAtsthyAttacchabdaM karmakarmasAmAnyamAtraM sarveShAmukthamityAdi pUrvavat /
tadetadyathoktaM nAma rUpaM karma trayamitaretarAshrayam, itaretarAbhivyaktikAraNam, itaretarapralayaM saMhataM tridaNDaviShTambhavat sadekam /
kenAtmanaikatvam? ityucyate - ayamAtmAyaM piNDaH kAryakaraNAtmasaN^ghAtaH tathAnnatraye vyAkhyAtaH'etanmayo vA ayamAtmA'ityAdinA;etAvaddhIdaM sarvaM vyAkR^itamavyAkR^itaM ca yaduta nAma rUpaM karmeti, AtmA u eko 'yaM kAryakaraNasaN^ghAtaH sannadhyAtmAdhibhUtAdhidaivabhAvena vyavasthitametadeva trayaM nAma rUpaM karmeti /
tadetadvakShyamANam /
amR^itaM satyenacchannamityetasya vAkyasyArthamAha - prANo vA amR^itaM karaNAtmako 'ntarupaShTambhaka AtmabhUto 'bhUto 'vinAshI;nAmarUpe satyaM kAryAtmake sharIrAvasthe;kriyAtmakastu prANastayorupaShTambhako bAhy bAhy AbhyAM sharIrAtmakAbhyAmupajanApAyadharmibhyAM martyAbhyAM channo 'prakAshIkR^itaH /
etadevasaMsArasatatvamavidyAviShayaM pradarshitam /
ata
UrdhvaM vidyAviShaya AtmAdhigantavya ithi caturthaM Arabhyate //3 // //

#<iti prathamAdhyAye ShaShThamukthabrAhmaNam //6//>#
